News

Soviet Russian Military Strength Statistics in the Far Eastern Crisis

The Army and Air Force Hold Supreme Authority

Over Three Million Soldiers Available for General Mobilization

Geneva News - According to reports collected here, Soviet Russian military strength holds supreme authority and is poised to become one of the most important factors in international affairs. At this year's disarmament conference, the Soviet Russian representative officially reported that the Soviet Russian standing army totaled 620,590 men. However, the representative did not specify whether this number included only the permanent Red Army or other troops as well. According to reliable semi-official sources, the Soviet Union has 1,178,000 people who can be mobilized for combat at any time. If the entire country is mobilized, 3.6 million soldiers can be obtained in a matter of weeks. Furthermore, according to the League of Nations' officially published annual report on national armaments, Soviet Russia conscripts 800,000 men each year. The training period is five full years. Among them, 200,000 join the standing Red Army, 200,000 are distributed to local military units, and the remaining 400,000 are inserted into various special military organizations. In addition, students from the Red Army's permanent military schools and semi-military special groups, such as the political police and Red Guards, are all included in the overall calculation. The size of the force is the largest in Europe, and the abundance of armaments is unmatched by other countries. The Red Army's Five-Year Plan projects that by 1935, the air force will have 5,000 aircraft, distributed among 62 air force regiments. News from the disarmament conference indicates that Soviet Russia currently has 2,000 aircraft. In addition, it is making large purchases of air force equipment from Italy, Czechoslovakia, and the Netherlands, worth over 10 million yuan. According to the Five-Year Military Plan, this year (1932), Soviet Russia's air force expansion should average 100 aircraft added each month. As for the Red Army soldiers' morale and technical skill, European military experts are full of praise. The excellence of the armaments is no less than that of any strong nation in the world. In general, a Red Army regiment has 2,867 rifles, 55 machine guns, 54 machine gun carriages, 6 field guns, and 6 heavy guns. Over the past two years, Soviet Russia has ordered 429 armored vehicles from Britain and Italy and purchased many aircraft parts from Germany and Sweden. Furthermore, according to Soviet Russian conscription laws, healthy young people, both men and women, between the ages of 19 and 20 must undergo preliminary military training for two months. After that, the term of service in the regular army is five years for those serving in the infantry, artillery, cavalry, or armored forces, with two years being continuous. In the air force, three years must be continuous, and in the navy, four years must be continuous. The 1932 Moscow military budget is 1,396,500,000 rubles, an increase of 271,500,000 rubles compared to 1931. Assuming that each ruble has a purchasing power of 50 cents in US dollars, the military expenditures of Russia and the United States are comparable. As for the navy, Russia cannot compare with the major naval powers, but Soviet Russia has 4 cruisers, 5 battleships, 24 destroyers, 13 submarines, and more than 10 other warships, all concentrated in the Black Sea, where they have created an overwhelming force. (World News Agency)

Soviet Russian Troops Mobilize

Actively Preparing for War

Elite Troops Assembled in the Far East

Tension in Northern Manchuria

Tokyo's "Hochi Shimbun" reports that recent Soviet Russian military actions towards Manchuria have become tense again, and rear defense preparations have gradually become concrete. Therefore, the rumor of war between Japan and Russia has revived. According to Russian reports, the total Soviet Russian force on the Russian-Manchurian border reaches 300,000 men, under the command of the Far Eastern Command in Irkutsk. Division headquarters have been established in five locations: Dauria, Vladivostok, Nikolaevsk, Khabarovsk, and Arkhara. Furthermore, naval and air bases have been established in Chita, Khabarovsk, and Irkutsk. Recently, large airfields in the vicinity of Voevodslava near the Korfovskaya Railway between Nikolaevsk and Pokranichny, Spasskoye, and Iman, as well as along the Russian-Korean border in Posiet have been completed, equipped with 150 aircraft. The current deployment of Russian troops in the Far East is as follows: (1) Vladivostok area: the Pacific 1st Division, the 3rd Verkhneudinsk Rifle Regiment, independent cavalry regiment, independent signals regiment, artillery battalion of the 3rd Rifle Regiment, engineering battalion, 1st Provisional Local Division, and students of the 3rd International Infantry School, etc.; (2) Nikolaevsk area: the 1st Chita Rifle Regiment, artillery battalion, 80th Cavalry Regiment, 85th Cavalry Regiment, heavy artillery regiment, independent signals platoon battalion, engineering battalion, etc.; (3) Khabarovsk area: the 2nd Pacific 1st Division, 4th Ussuriysk Rifle Regiment, 6th Khabarovsk Rifle Regiment, artillery battalion, 1st Cavalry Regiment, 2nd Cavalry Regiment, independent cavalry regiment, heavy artillery regiment, railway battalion, engineering company, seaplane squadron, river fleet, etc.; (4) Irkutsk area: the 35th Division, 36th Division, 105th Rifle Regiment, 103rd Rifle Regiment, independent cavalry regiment, independent signals battalion, independent engineering company, artillery regiment, railway regiment, land-based air squadron, armored vehicles, etc., within the Far Eastern Military Headquarters; (5) Dauriya area: the 74th Cavalry Regiment, independent 5th Cavalry Brigade, Buryat Regiment, Mongolian Regiment, independent engineering battalion, armored train, etc.; (6) Blagoveshchensk area: the 5th Heilongjiang Rifle Regiment, artillery battalion, independent signals company, others unknown; (7) Rastorguyevo area: the 2nd Nerchinsk Rifle Regiment, artillery battalion, etc.; (8) Chita area: the 35th Division, land-based air squadron; (9) Spasskoye area: the 86th Cavalry Regiment, armored vehicle squadron, 108th Sretensk Rifle Regiment, 107th Pogranichny Rifle Regiment, Abakan artillery regiment, 104th Verkhneudinsk Rifle Regiment, 73rd Nerchinsk Cavalry Regiment, etc. Russia's elite forces have been completely concentrated in the Far East. The strategic focus is on the Manchouli border, the opposite bank of the Heihe River, and the vicinity of Pokranichny. In recent days, the Russian military has concentrated a large force of 200,000 men in the areas of Arkhara, Blagoveshchensk, and Arkhara on the opposite bank of the Heihe River, which has drawn considerable attention from the government authorities.

Tokyo's "Jiji Shimpo" reported that on the 7th, a German Berlin reporter interviewed War Minister Araki. Araki made the following statement on the Russian issue: Japan has no intention of infringing upon the rights and interests of Soviet Russia, nor do Japanese troops intend to enter Soviet Russian territory or instigate White Russians to resist Red Russia. Now, the Soviet Union is concentrating a large army on the border, and some communists are clamoring for Japan to start a war, making relations between the two countries increasingly unfavorable. However, Japan maintains that if Soviet Russia does not attack the Manchurian border, there will be no danger. Therefore, it is hoped that Soviet Russian troops will withdraw and not be influenced by propaganda and instigation.

Volunteer Army Recaptures Shulan and Wuchang

Heavy Casualties Suffered by Japanese Troops in the Battle of Xinlitun

Many Japanese Soldiers Desert Due to the Inability to Endure Hard Battles

Suifenhe correspondence: From July 5, the Volunteer Army forces led by Gong Changhai, Feng Zhanhai, and others moved towards Wuchang and Shulan. Gong's main force engaged in fierce battles with Japanese troops in Xinlitun, Yushu, and then concentrated in Shanhetun, south of Wuchang. Feng's forces concentrated in Tuqiaozi (25 li from Xinlitun). Zhao Wenbin's Volunteer Army concentrated along the Lalin River, waiting for an opportunity to strike at the Japanese and the puppet Ji army led by Liu in Wuokeshu. As a result, the Japanese troops did not dare to advance deeply. However, on the 5th, Japanese aircraft reconnoitered the front lines and reported that Gong Changhai's army of 4,000, with the Big Sword Society and Red Spear Society in the rear, was approaching the northern suburbs of Shulan County, only 20 li or so away. The Nakamura unit of the Japanese army in Xinlitun rushed to that area to block them. However, at the same time, Feng Zhanhai's main force of over 3,000 moved from Xiushuidianzi towards the puppet capital of Changchun. The Japanese 14th Division also dispatched troops on the morning of the 6th to deploy defenses along the Jichang Road to Jilin. As for Li Haiching's cavalry force of about 2,000 men, they supported Gong and Feng's armies, protruding between Xiagutai and Tumenling on the Jichang Road. Although they had not yet advanced to the vicinity of the route, Jichang and Jiyuan were already feeling threatened. Furthermore, the Volunteer Army led by Yang Wenlin moved towards Wuchang on the morning of the 5th to divert the Japanese and puppet Ji army forces. Therefore, the Japanese and puppet army's 1st Guard Brigade in Wuokeshu and Yushu County rushed to Wuchang to block them on the afternoon of the 5th. However, the Volunteer Army marched very quickly and, without waiting for the Japanese and puppet armies to arrive, had already captured Shulan and Wuchang.

Recalling the fierce battle of Xinlitun on July 1, the Volunteer Army attacked from three directions. Japanese aircraft dropped bombs from the air, but the Volunteer Army was not afraid and fought fiercely for nine hours. The Japanese Okawa company was completely annihilated. The company commander, Okawa, was stabbed to death by the Red Spear Society. More than 70 soldiers, officers, and non-commissioned officers were captured. As a result, the Japanese were discouraged. It was heard that the Funabashi regiment suffered the greatest losses. An armored vehicle also became stuck in the mud and was destroyed by the Volunteer Army. Afterwards, the Japanese announced that the Red Spear Society fought bare-armed and used iron spears about three chi long, with dozens or hundreds of people in a team. During battle, they shouted killing cries that shook the heavens and the earth. With each killing cry, dozens of warriors leaped forward. Although the Japanese used machine guns to fire upon them, they did not retreat. Therefore, the Japanese who were injured were all stabbed by this kind of weapon. As for the Okawa company, a lieutenant commander named Jin fled back to his unit after being captured by the Volunteer Army. He reported to his unit that the Volunteer Army was organized, currently centered on Feng Zhanhai, with Feng as the commander-in-chief and Gong Changhai as the deputy commander. Yao Bingqian, Zhao Wenbin, and Yang Wenlin each served as brigade commanders and cavalry and infantry commanders. They had already issued grand pronouncements, vowing to seize Hsinking (Changchun) and advance on Jilin. The total number of people who set out this time was estimated to be over 10,000, lacking only ammunition.

The Volunteer Army specializes in fighting away from railway lines, so the Japanese army, despite having sharp weapons and occupied transportation facilities, cannot use them. During the hot nights, they camp in the wilderness, where mosquitoes swarm. The Japanese soldiers cannot endure it. For example, the soldiers of the Funabashi regiment have their faces and bodies stung by mosquitoes, causing many ulcers like morphine needle pricks. Furthermore, due to camping in the wild and inadequate supplies, many suffer from typhus. Most of the soldiers of the 10th Division were recruited from Okayama Prefecture and enlisted in 1930. Half of them are due to be discharged in May and November of this year. Because they are stationed far away, they cannot be discharged and there are rumors of extending their service period. Therefore, many Japanese soldiers are deserting out of disappointment. The Japanese military has already strictly prohibited this, but those who flee still flee. There is news that Li Du's righteous army recaptured Fujin on July 3. When the Japanese army in Harbin heard the news, they originally wanted to send troops, but the 6th, 10th, and 14th Divisions were afraid to send troops far away, so they have not yet set out. (July 6)

The Three Provinces Bandit Suppression Headquarters Establishes Party and Government Committees

Each of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Establishes Party and Government Conferences

Hankou Correspondence: Commander-in-Chief Chiang, in order to carry out a large-scale bandit suppression in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, and regarding local rehabilitation, originally planned to establish an administrative affairs bureau to be responsible for handling affairs. In Hubei Province, a Party and Government Committee was to be established as an advisory body. It was also heard that Zhang Qun was internally designated as the director of the Administrative Affairs Bureau, and Zhang Nanxian, Wen Juntian, and others were appointed as members of the Party and Government Committee. After further consideration, the establishment of the Administrative Affairs Bureau was temporarily postponed, and only the Party and Government Committee was established to assist the Headquarters in guiding and supervising the implementation and improvement of Party affairs and politics in the bandit suppression areas of the three provinces. Party and government conferences will be established in Henan, Hubei, and Anhui provinces, roughly similar to the precedent of the Jiangxi Provincial Party Affairs Committee last year, but the organization is more complete. The organizational regulations were promulgated by the Headquarters on the 11th, and the original text is as follows: (Article 1) For the purpose of guiding and supervising the implementation and improvement of Party and government affairs in the bandit suppression areas of the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, the Commander-in-Chief of the Bandit Suppression specially establishes a Party and Government Committee to assist in handling matters. The matters handled by the Party and Government Committee shall be submitted to the Commander-in-Chief for approval and executed by order of the Commander-in-Chief. (Article 2) The Party and Government Committee shall be established at the location of the Bandit Suppression Headquarters. (Article 3) The Party and Government Committee shall have nine members. (Article 4) The Party and Government Committee shall have the following departments: 1. Office of the Standing Committee; 2. Supervision Department; 3. Party Affairs Guidance Department; 4. Political Affairs Guidance Department. (Article 5) The Office of the Standing Committee shall have three members of the Standing Committee. Each department shall have one director and two deputy directors. The directors and deputy directors of each department shall be concurrently held by the members respectively. The Standing Committee members shall concurrently serve as the directors of each department. In the event of an accident involving the director, one of the deputy directors of that department shall be designated to act as the director and member of the Standing Committee. (Article 6) The Office of the Standing Committee shall have one chief secretary and two secretaries who, under the command of the Standing Committee members, shall be in charge of the documents, accounting, general affairs, meeting convocation, minutes of meetings, and other matters not belonging to each department. (Article 7) The Supervision Department shall have one secretary and two clerks who, under the command of the chief officer, shall be in charge of the following matters: 1. Supervising the implementation of the cleaning up and rehabilitation measures in various places, and examining the qualifications for the appointment of officials at all levels; 2. Investigating the integrity, diligence, laziness, and all service conditions of Party, government, and military personnel in the bandit suppression areas; 3. Conducting spot checks of household registration and inspections of local defense forces; 4. Collecting petitions and appeals from local people or organizations, and all matters requiring secret investigation; 5. Investigating accusations of corruption, local bullies, and bandits using public office for personal revenge or personal gain; 6. Investigating the arbitrary requisitioning by various troops in the locality, or the shielding of the private transport of opium, salt, and other goods; 7. Formulating regulations for rewards and punishments for Party, government, and military personnel, and strictly implementing them; 8. Determining whether accused or reported personnel should be handed over to the military law office or ordinary court. (Article 8) The Party Affairs Guidance Department shall have one secretary and two clerks who, under the command of the chief officer, shall be in charge of the following matters: 1. Planning and guiding the organization of Party affairs in the bandit suppression areas, and all related activities; 2. Planning and guiding the organization, training, reorganization, and all activities of mass organizations in the bandit suppression areas; 3. Planning and guiding propaganda and general social education in the bandit suppression areas; 4. Utilizing aircraft, broadcasting, and radio, and planning and guiding all propaganda methods; 5. Specifying and issuing bandit suppression slogans and all printed materials; 6. Resolving disputes over Party affairs in the bandit suppression areas, and promoting close cooperation between Party departments at all levels and the government, as well as with local people. (Article 9) The Political Affairs Guidance Department shall have one secretary and five clerks who, under the command of the chief officer, shall be in charge of the following matters: 1. Formulating laws and regulations related to bandit suppression; 2. Supervising household registration and the implementation and reorganization of the Baojia system; 3. Reorganizing and training local security teams; 4. Regulating and training local defense forces and all mass self-defense organizations; 5. Reviewing and appointing or removing officers of security teams and local defense forces; 6. Repairing city walls in various counties and constructing defense towers in selected areas; 7. Preventing communication, installing telephones, roads, and completing all transportation networks; 8. Guiding and supervising all local clean-up measures, promoting self-government, and rural revitalization. (Article 10) The office and each department may, depending on the complexity of the affairs, establish a number of staff members and clerks. The rules for dividing shares and handling affairs in each office and department, as well as the quota of personnel, shall be determined separately. (Article 11) When one of the following circumstances occurs in the matters in charge of each department, a proposal shall be submitted to the Party and Government Committee for discussion: 1. The proposed plan has the nature of laws and regulations; 2. There is a common relationship between the various offices and departments; 3. Each department considers the circumstances to be more serious. The meetings of the Party and Government Committee shall be convened by the Standing Committee members. (Article 12) The Party and Government Committee shall establish the following three provincial Party and government conferences: 1. Hubei Party and Government Conference; 2. Henan Party and Government Conference; 3. Anhui Party and Government Conference. (Article 13) The provincial Party and government conferences shall be composed of the following personnel, collectively referred to as members of the Party and Government Conference of a certain province: 1. Members of the Party and Government Committee; 2. The chairman and members of the government of each province; 3. Members of the Party headquarters and special city Party headquarters of each province; 4. Personnel who are well-versed in the Party, government, and military situation of each province, and are specially designated by the Commander-in-Chief. (Article 14) The provincial Party and government conferences shall be convened according to the orders of the Commander-in-Chief. (Article 15) When the provincial Party and government conferences are convened, the Commander-in-Chief shall designate three to five members to form the presidium. The secretariat of the Party and Government Conference shall, under the orders of the presidium, be in charge of the documents and all affairs in the meeting, and shall be concurrently handled by the staff of the various offices and departments of the Party and Government Committee. (Article 16) The main duties of the provincial Party and government conferences are as follows: 1. Reporting on the actual situation of Party and government affairs and the current state of soldiers and bandits in each province; 2. Proposals for the improvement or promotion of Party and government affairs and all plans related to bandit suppression in each province; 3. Other matters submitted by the Commander-in-Chief for discussion. The resolutions of the foregoing matters shall be submitted to the Commander-in-Chief for approval and implementation. (Article 17) The rules of procedure for the Party and government conferences shall be determined separately. (Article 18) These regulations shall be implemented from the date of approval by the Commander-in-Chief of the Bandit Suppression.

It is heard that the Standing Committee members and members of the Party and Government Committee, as well as the directors of each department, have all been internally designated, and will be announced in the next few days. As for the convocation of the county magistrate conference of various counties in Hubei Province, they have successively arrived at the headquarters to report. Chiang Kai-shek originally planned to meet with fifteen people every day from the 11th to inquire about the political affairs, bandit situation, disaster situation, embankment works, local defense, disaster relief, and other matters in each county, and complete the meetings in four days, and then schedule a meeting. Because Chiang Kai-shek felt unwell, he did not meet with them on the 11th. The conference period has not yet been determined. (July 11)

(August 8)

The Flood on the Grand Canal Rages; Summer Defense Funds Still Not in Place

A Conversation with the Director of the Grand Canal Engineering Bureau

Yangzhou Correspondence: The banks of the Grand Canal north of the Yangtze River were breached in 27 places last autumn, totaling more than 900 feet. The loss of life and property of the people, and the relief efforts to raise donations, were certainly substantial. The remission of land taxes in the flooded counties and the funding for repairing the dikes cost the public six to seven million or more. This year's summer tides are particularly high. Although the gates of the various dams along the Grand Canal have been opened early, not only can the river water not be discharged, but the tides are backflowing very rapidly. Therefore, the water level of the Grand Canal is rising day by day. Residents along the coast are all terrified, fearing that last autumn's disaster will be repeated this year. Therefore, they are running around calling for help, hoping to prevent it before it happens. Recently, I met Xu Dingkang, the newly appointed director of the Grand Canal Engineering Bureau. According to him, regarding the issue of governing the Grand Canal, he said that recently, because there are no concrete measures for funding, the Grand Canal project is very worrying. Therefore, what needs to be resolved urgently today includes four items: (1) The old and new land tax (about 300,000 yuan per year) should be specially preserved, and cannot be used until the accumulation is sufficient for harbor management and river dredging. (2) The old dikes are now in disrepair and the new works are not solid. According to the summer defense funds in the summer of the tenth year of the Republic of China, 180,000 yuan was still used. This year's summer defense funds will not be enough to overcome this difficult situation unless 200,000 yuan is raised. The provincial government has agreed to spend 50,000 yuan from the old and new land tax to cover the summer defense expenses. This amount is not enough, and it seems inappropriate to use the land tax in the first step. (3) The bureau's operating expenses, as well as the three sections of Jiangdu, Gaobao, Huaip, and Pizhou, together with the radio station, require more than 8,000 yuan per month. This money should be spent from the provincial administrative expenses, and there is no reason to transfer the land tax. (4) There are too few engineering personnel. Without adequate treatment, it is impossible to find suitable talents. The above four items have been submitted to the provincial government for review and approval. This year's water level is no less than last year. If the above cannot be done, then long-term plans will be even more difficult. Although personal sacrifices are made, it will not help the Grand Canal water disaster.

Local Correspondence

Kunshan

The Worrying Spread of Cholera in Kunshan: Cholera has been prevalent in Kunshan recently, and those who contract the disease die in the evening if they catch it in the morning, which is quite alarming. The speed of its spread is unstoppable. Bacheng Township is the most severely affected area, and those who contract the disease die before they can be treated. Although the epidemic prevention efforts include doctors from various hospitals and doctors and boy scouts sent by the Shanghai War Zone Rehabilitation Committee, who are injecting epidemic prevention shots for all sectors and disinfecting in various places, the epidemic is still spreading. Therefore, dozens of people in the urban area have contracted the disease and died in the past few days. Although there is a proposal to set up an epidemic prevention station, it has not yet been realized. In addition, the weather was hot and humid for the past two days, and the epidemic has become more severe, and the consequences will be disastrous. The Provincial Water Police Capture Two Thieves: The leader of the 12th team of the Kunshan Provincial Water Police, Ge Xiancai, captured two bandits, Wu and Lin, in Luzhajia Port the night before last night. In addition to informing the county by telegram, Li, the director of the Provincial Security Office, has also sent Director Liang and Ke Yuan Xu to Wuxi to press for payments. The county government now has a sigh of helplessness.

Donations Collected to Accommodate Refugees from Yili: The provinces of Jiangsu are suffering from poor harvests year after year, and are also experiencing major floods, resulting in famished people everywhere, which is unbearable to see. More than 1,000 refugees from Yixing and Liyang have arrived in the Sanniqiao area outside the North Gate of Wuxi in recent days, divided into more than 20 small teams, with hungry and exhausted faces, begging along the way, and sleeping in the streets at night. Currently, Shi Xiangchen and He Weizhou, members of the Jiangwan Red Swastika Society, are raising funds to temporarily accommodate them in places such as the Yansheng Hall of the Fucheng Chenghuang Temple, and will then find ways to send them back to their hometowns.

Changzhou

Weicun Sailing Ship Robbed En Route: The Weicun sailing ship departed from the city to the countryside on the 9th. At around 12 o'clock at night, when passing under the Lianjiang Bridge north of the Desheng River Yang Bridge, six or seven armed bandits suddenly boarded the ship and robbed all the goods, cash, and passengers' clothes and silver, totaling about 500 yuan. Afterwards, the nearby police force captured two suspected bandits, Lao Wang and Xiao Liu, who are being interrogated. The owners also reported the case to the county on the 11th, requesting an arrest.

The Qingyunfang Illegal Drug Pill Manufacturing Operation is Cracked: Fang Weizhou, the director of the Public Security Bureau of Wu County, dispatched officers to investigate Qin Abaao of No. 8 Qingyunfang in the city, who was privately manufacturing drug pills. He immediately ordered supervisor Huang Yongshou to search the place yesterday (11th). As a result, three pieces of machinery for manufacturing drug pills, five packages of raw materials, and pill guns were found. Qin Abaao was also captured on the spot and taken to the bureau for preliminary examination. Today (12th), he was transferred to the county court for interrogation.

Nantong

The Perpetrator of the Filial Murder Case is Sentenced to Death: The case of the nephew strangling his uncle, which shocked the entire county, has been verified by the court after exhumation. The Criminal Court announced the verdict on the 11th. The principal offender, Yang Guangchong, and the accomplices, Li Rentang and Cai Changyuan, were all found guilty of conspiring to commit murder and were sentenced to death.

Gaoyou

The Seventeen-Life Case is Adjudicated: Bai Weixiang, the head of Gongtian Township in the county's second district, was previously accused by Xu Yongnian and other villagers of shooting and killing seventeen poor people when the dike breached last autumn. The trial of the case was concluded a few days ago. It is now heard that the county government has ruled yesterday that Bai Weixiang was sentenced to five years of imprisonment for instigating injury resulting in the death of seventeen people who drowned. Bai Changxu, Bai Changkun, Zhang Mingluo, and Zhang Changfu were acquitted.

Xiaoshan

The victim is now in critical condition, and the adulterer Cai Yinsheng has fled. Hu is now seriously injured, and it is unknown whether his life can be saved.

Important News

Conference of Presidents of Colleges and Above

Discussing University Administration, Teacher Treatment and Other Issues

Nanjing, December 12th - The presidents of national colleges and universities above junior college level continued to meet at the Ministry of Education on the afternoon of the 12th, with Zhu Jia as chairman, to discuss the University Organization Law. 1. The issue of university branch campuses was maintained as originally planned. 2. The organizational structure of the university's administrative department has been modified. 3. The classification and titles of university teachers have been modified. 4. The organization and powers of the school affairs committee have been changed. In addition, issues such as the length of study, degree issues, special student issues, qualifications, appointment, and treatment of university teachers were also discussed.

Datong University Moves Back to Zhongshan Road

Datong University on Zhongshan Road in West Shanghai, which had moved to its old school building on Jiaozhou Road after the outbreak of the Sino-Japanese War, is now returning to Zhongshan Road on July 16th and 17th as order in West Shanghai has long returned to normal. The summer school is scheduled to register from July 29th and classes will begin on August 1st. Autumn freshmen will be admitted on August 9th and 10th. Students who have not completed their studies in the autumn of the 20th year will have them completed at the school on September 8th, 9th, and 13th; no make-up sessions will be held after the deadline. Autumn registration for the school year will begin on September 15th. In order to facilitate students' admission to higher education, the high school and junior high school will add spring starter classes from the next semester. Kindergarten normal school will be listed as one of the high school courses from the next semester. Teaching and organization will be more convenient. In addition, the school's newly equipped science laboratory and library are very complete.

Minutes of the First Meeting of the China Football Association Committee

The Summer Football Inter-Trade Cup Regulations were Approved

The Shanghai China Football Association plans to hold the competition season earlier this year, and has specially hired experts to form a committee to prepare and proceed. At the first meeting of the association the night before, those who attended were Jiang Xiangqing, Feng Jianwei, Le Xiurong, He Chunhui, Ma Detai, Zhou Jiaqi (on behalf of). Zhou Jiaqi, Feng Jianwei was elected as chairman at the meeting to discuss the regulations for the two competitions. Excerpts from the resolutions are as follows:

(1) It was decided to hold the Summer Football League and the Inter-Trade Cup from August 13th.

(2) The Summer Football League is limited to 16 teams. Only former members of the (China) three groups of the China Football Association and teams with considerable strength that have been approved by this committee may join the league.

(3) The Inter-Trade Cup adopts a knockout system. The championship is not divided into grades. The winner is the championship team of the cup competition.

(4) The competition time is stipulated as 60 minutes, with the first and second halves lasting 30 minutes and a 10-minute break.

(5) Registration starts on July 18th and ends on July 31st.

(6) Each team is limited to four substitutes in the competition.

(7) Dong Zhenyuan donated a large silver cup for the league. The name of the championship team each year will be engraved on the cup and kept by the team for one year.

(8) The award for the Inter-Trade Cup is a silver cup donated by the Taiping Insurance Company. The team that wins two years first will permanently keep the cup.

(9) The back of each team's jersey must have a number that is at least six inches square for identification purposes.

(10) The registration fee for each team in the cup competition is five yuan.

(11) A number of regulations related to the Inter-Trade Cup were agreed as follows: (1) Only amateur teams organized by employees of businesses in the commercial sector and independent organizations in the political and industrial sectors are allowed to join this competition. Apprentice teams and teams organized by sports organizations are not allowed to join. (2) Each team joining the competition should use the name of the business or organization to which the team belongs as the team name. (3) Players must have at least three months of service qualification before they can represent the business or political and industrial organization team and join the competition. (4) The registration of each team must be signed and responsible by the manager or director of the business or organization to prove that the players in the team are all employees of the business or organization for more than three months and are amateur athletes. (5) If the match is not decided within the stipulated time, the match will be extended by 20 minutes (i.e., the field will be changed every 10 minutes). (Note) Detailed regulations for the league and the Inter-Trade Cup will be announced later.

A Record of Huiberdeng's Failure to Show Strength

Where is the Glory of the Tennis King?

(London Correspondence) In the Huiberdeng Conference, the failure of the Tennis King, Ke Xian, to Kao Linsi is regarded as a strange thing. The situation of the game is recorded as follows.

On the second day of the Huiberdeng Conference, the sun was setting. This astonishing discovery was that Ke Xian, a champion player, was defeated by Kao Linsi, a former British Taibei player, 6 to 2, 8 to 6, 0 to 6, and 6 to 3. At this time last year, Ke Xian also lost to Xia Bo on the first day of the conference at this first court. This year, he made a comeback, intending to restore the glory of his past in Huiberdeng.

In Kao Linsi, no one regarded him as an opponent of Ke Xian. Therefore, Kao Linsi, a Scotsman, was a doubles player himself.

As soon as the game started, Ke Xian treated him with an indifferent attitude, because he had to use the first set as practice. Kao Linsi then rose steadily, 4 to 1, 5 to 2, and Ke Xian gave up the last game again.

A good show then opened. Ke Xian was very dissatisfied with the linesman. When a ball came, the linesman did not see it and could not decide. The referee decided it. This happened again and again. Ke Xian asked to change it. Bi Xuepo finally left, which was the third game of the second set.

The battle was obviously fierce, and Ke Xian tried his best to win back this second set, but Kao Linsi knew it deeply and continued to make progress.

The servers all won, and Kao took the lead with five to four. At this point, Ke Xian showed his ability to shoot fiercely at both corners with amazing force and won two games in a row. Kao Linsi did not give in and fought back with a cannonball serve, winning a game and hitting twice more. This second set also belonged to Kao Linsi.

The wind and rain filled the court. This shocking news shocked the world. The 6,000 spectators did not expect the great king to be defeated by a doubles player.

In the third set, Ke Xian won two games, and Kao let him go and completely gave up six games to regroup. Kao won first, and Ke also won back. Then, Kao showed his colors, attacking left and right, and slashing fiercely into the depths of the corners. Ke Xian fought to the death and finally lost, three to one, and four to one.

Ke made another desperate battle and won two games. But would Kao Linsi give up?

Kao Linsi broke Ke Xian's serve, an amazing overhead pressure and slash, and Kao won five to three.

In the last game, Ke Xian almost won, but in the third decisive point, Kao Linsi served fiercely and then slashed, and Ke Xian was defeated.

The Past and Present of the World Games (8)

(8) A Review of Athletics Competitions at the Past Sessions (Part 1)

The first session was held in 1896 in Athens, the capital of Greece. There were only 12 athletics events. The results were immature and not as good as the current records in China. The track events were only 100 meters, 400 meters, 800 meters, 1,500 meters, and the marathon (according to the marathon, the course is 42 kilometers and 195 meters, which is 26 miles and 385 yards). There was a 110-meter high hurdle but no low hurdle. In terms of field events, in addition to the currently popular ones, only javelin and chain clock were missing. The iron disc result was only 95 feet and 7.5 inches, 100 meters was 12 seconds, 400 meters was 54.2 seconds, and the high hurdle was 17.6 seconds. As a result of the competition, except for the 800 meters and 1,500 meters won by the United Kingdom and the marathon won by Greece, the rest belonged to the United States.

The second session was held in 1900 in Paris, the capital of France. The number of athletics events increased from 12 to 22. The track events ranged from 60 meters to 1,500 meters. The hurdles were divided into 110 meters, 200 meters, and 400 meters, and 2,500 meters and 4,000 meters were added to the jumping beach. Field events added 16-pound chain clock and standing high jump, standing long jump, and standing triple jump. The results have greatly improved, such as the 49.4 seconds of the 400-meter American Dragon, the high and low hurdle of Clasin (USA), and the 167 feet and 4 inches of the chain clock of Flangnagan, etc., all became immortal figures in Yalin Sikhs. As a result of the competition, the United Kingdom won three firsts, France and Hungary each won one first, and the remaining champions belonged to the United States.

The third session: After the United States won two consecutive victories, the interest became more intense. The third session was requested to be held in St. Louis, USA in 1904. The number of American players who joined was very enthusiastic, one because of the local relationship and the other because of the efforts over the years. The results have improved by leaps and bounds. This session can be called an exhibition of the total achievements of the United States alone. Other countries have been defeated by the wind. The athletics program is the same as the second session, except for one item of 4,000-meter jumping beach. American players monopolized the championship of all programs, which can be called one of the most glorious pages in history. Among them, such as La Erfuluosi's 48 feet and 7 inches of 16-pound shot put results, Pulinston's 24 feet of long jump, Flangnagan's re-winning of chain throwing, and Hill Meng's hurdle jumping are still deeply imprinted in the minds of athletes in various countries in recent times. Swimming pool of this World Games

The fourth session: This session was held again in Athens, Greece in 1906. The results have declined greatly. The field events canceled the standing triple jump and chain hammer, and added javelin and five sports trails. In terms of competition, it still returned to the program of the first session. The United States still accounted for the victory, winning a total of eleven championships, followed by the United Kingdom, France, Sweden, and Canada. It was found that this meeting was ten years apart from the first session. The Greek brain committee proposed that it should still follow the ancient Greek method and hold a meeting every four years, which was unanimously resolved.

However, the fifth session has been decided to be held in 1908, which is not convenient to delay.

Local News

Sanbei Shanghai River Vessel

Wu Xing Ran Aground and Sinks

All Crew and Passengers Fortunately Rescued

This year, merchant ships in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River often have accidents. First, there was the Yibin of Jiejang, and then there was the Wanliu of Taikoo, both of which ran aground and sank. Recently, the Wuxing vessel of the Sanbei Company also ran aground due to accidentally running aground in the middle of its voyage from Chongqing. The Shanghai office is preparing to salvage it. The details obtained from the reporter's investigation are recorded as follows.

The surging water caused the disaster. The Sanbei Company's Shangjiang vessels, which travel between Chongqing and Yichang, include Wuxing and Fuyang. On the 7th of this month, the Wuxing vessel carried cargo and passengers from Chongqing to Yichang. When it reached the 70th area near Yunyang, the place where the former Yibin Wanliu sank, it was on the afternoon of the 8th. Since the water in the Sichuan River has risen recently, the eastward flow is very turbulent. River vessels usually reduce their speed when going downstream to avoid accidents. However, the Wuxing was driven by the turbulent flow, and the hull lost its driving force, so it rushed to the reef with the current. I wanted to

It was too late to save the car, and the hull crashed into the reef. The bottom of the ship broke immediately.

Damage to the machinery. The place where the Wuxing ran aground was in the engine room of the middle compartment. The hull was pierced by the reef, and the river water rushed into the compartment. In an instant, the water depth in the machine room was five or six feet, and the engine was submerged in the water. The boiler went out and could not move. Before long, the first compartment was also damaged by the reef, and water also rushed in, and the hull sank downward. The situation was very dangerous.

Passengers rescued: At the time of the accident, the passengers in the ship were very panicked and went to the deck to escape for their lives. Seeing this situation, the shipowner immediately released a distress signal and pulled the life-saving echo. Fortunately, the Jiahe wheel of Yihua Yanghang passed by upstream and heard the police signal, so it drove to help rescue. The small sampan was sent to rescue all the passengers on the Wuxing wheel and sent them to Yichang to land.

The hull sank: After receiving the telegram about the Wuxing accident, the Shanghai Sanbei Company received a telegram from Ren Yuqing, the director of the Yichang branch, yesterday, saying that after the Wuxing ran aground, the machine room was flooded first, and then the head compartment was flooded. The hull was heavily loaded and flooded again. At first, three-quarters of the ship sank in the river. Now, because the water is turbulent and heavy, the entire ship has sunk into the river. Fortunately, it is搁 on the reef, and although it has sunk, it can still be salvaged.

Salvage in progress: Yesterday, the Shanghai Bureau has sent an urgent telegram to the Yi Branch Bureau, ordering Ren Ziqing to first send a ship to the place where the Wuxing accident occurred nearby, and try to take out the goods and other important items in the ship that can be taken out, and reduce the load on the ship. On the one hand, it also ordered workers and technicians to be sent from Yichang with cement to the location to try to repair the hole in Wuxing. Then, wait for the water to fall shallow before carrying out the salvage procedure. It is found that the ship has a net tonnage of 300 tons and has been sailing on the Sichuan River for about seven years. The estimated value of the ship and cargo is about 400,000 yuan.

The Municipal Government's Attitude Towards Labor Disputes

Hoping for Mutual Understanding

Yu Hongjun, Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, announced the Municipal Government's attitude towards labor disputes. He said that the Municipal Government hopes that both labor and management can understand each other and adopt a spirit of coordination and cooperation. If the conditions proposed by the workers are indeed reasonable, the capitalists should also understand the workers' living standards and improve them. If the conditions proposed by the workers are indeed impossible for the facts, it is difficult to force the capitalists to fulfill them. In short, both parties should be calm and not fight for emotional reasons. If the capitalists indeed deprive workers of their livelihood and dismiss them without cause, or the workers deliberately cause trouble, the Municipal Government will handle it fairly.

Mediation scheduled to continue this afternoon

The trade association is discussing ways to prevent the strike. The various situations are recorded below:

Putianle and others strike. The guild is trying to prevent a general strike. The National Medicine Industry Association specially discussed ways to prevent a general strike yesterday and convened an extraordinary emergency executive committee. Committee members Sun Wen'an, Guo Baosheng, Tong Guangfu, Zhuang Meitang, Niu Hegao, Cen Qisheng, Cen Binghuang, Chen Chuxiang, Zhou Qiansheng, Cen Zhiliang, Zhang Meian, Zhang Hongran, Li Kangnian, etc. attended. However, these four stores will allocate 10% of their daily business income to donate to the union's strike fund. This kind of plan seems to be for the convenience of patients buying medicine, but in reality, it is a collusion between labor and management, privately benefiting themselves. In order to clean up the scum in the industry, the association will take extremely severe measures to deal with the treacherous behavior of these four pharmacies in order to counter them. Furthermore, a large group of unemployed workers plans to petition the trade association tomorrow afternoon. It is said that the association has decided not to pay attention to them.

The party and government talks. The Municipal Social Bureau convened the second talk between labor and management at 1:00 PM yesterday. Cen Zhiliang and Zhuang Meitang of the National Medicine Industry Association, Shi Qintang, Fang Qingjian, Zhao Zhenhui, and Yuan Pinzhang of the Pharmaceutical Workers' Union, Wang Manyun, director of the People's Training Section of the Municipal Party Headquarters, and Xu Yefu, the third section chief of the Social Bureau, attended. Chaired by Xu Yefu, the chairman first reported that today's meeting is a continuation of the previous talks. If both parties have any opinions, they can openly state them to each other. However, in the past, labor strikes in the pharmaceutical industry have emerged one after another. At a time when the Communist Party is active, it is hoped that both sides can understand each other and resolve the issue as soon as possible. This is what the government authorities earnestly hope. Now report on the results of the last talks and the agreed-upon methods. Then the labor representatives stated that: (1) Regarding the Feng Cunren Tang issue, the management is now asking private accountant Pan to investigate, which is not appropriate. Please ask your bureau to appoint an accountant to show fairness. (2) Before the labor-management agreement is revised, the management must not arbitrarily violate the agreement. The resolution passed by the industry association a few days ago stated that the union cannot interfere with replacement workers in other venues in the future. According to the union, it has not been resolved by the representative assembly. It can be seen that the replacement worker issue is being manipulated by a few in the union. The management stated that the reason for the Feng Cunren matter is that the employees are very eager for bonuses, so they asked accountant Pan to investigate. In order to quickly resolve the issue before the investigation is completed, each person will temporarily borrow one month's salary. Regarding the replacement worker issue, it should be handled by the management themselves as in the previous talks. As for the method, it can be modified and handled appropriately.

Mediation to continue today. The labor representatives put forward simple methods: (1) Give each person a bonus of three months' salary. Otherwise, please ask your bureau to extract the books and appoint an accountant to check the accounts. (2) The loss fee during the strike period will be paid by the management at 33 yuan per day. (3) The replacement workers will be implemented immediately. If the management can accept the above three points, they can resume work immediately. The management replied: (1) Feng Cunren has not made any money. The request for three months cannot be rashly allowed. (2) The accounts are being checked by accountants Pan and Hu. The labor representatives' request cannot be agreed to. (3) The loss cannot be allowed. (4) The replacement worker issue is an entire decree. Finally, the chairman ordered both parties to negotiate and resolve the issue with each other tonight (that is, yesterday). If it can be resolved, work will resume tomorrow. If the reconciliation fails, mediation will continue tomorrow (that is, today) at 1:00 PM until 7:00 PM before adjourning. However, it is said that labor and management negotiated a reconciliation on their own last night, but there were still no results, so mediation must continue today.

Employees will hold a general meeting. All members of the Pharmaceutical Workers' Union requested the union to convene a general meeting of members to decide on a countermeasure. A reporter from New Sound News met with Fang Qinghe, director of the Pharmaceutical Workers' Union, yesterday.

According to him, it has now been decided to hold a city-wide general meeting of members at the Yaowang Temple in Xiaonanmen at 1:00 PM on the 17th, but whether it will be held on time depends on the decision of the joint meeting of the union group on the 14th.

Electric Power Company Explains the Truth About the Labor Unrest

More than one hundred dismissed workers

Will still be hired when there is an opportunity

The various situations of the labor unrest at the Shanghai Electric Power Company have been repeatedly reported in previous newspapers. However, according to the company, the trend of the labor unrest is not as serious as rumored. The company's acting manager, Hillert, told reporters yesterday that since the autumn of last year, the company had discussed dismissing more than one hundred workers due to poor business. Later, it was predicted that business might recover this spring, and the existing workers would not be enough, so the company retained the work of more than one hundred workers last winter. Unexpectedly, since the Sino-Japanese war in Shanghai, the company's business has not only failed to recover, but has deteriorated. Therefore, in early June of this year, the company implemented the dismissal of more than one hundred workers. However, the company's door is still open. As soon as there is an opportunity, the company will still hire those one hundred workers.

The conflict. All the workers of the Anlu Cotton Mill, although the Municipal Social Bureau has mediated repeatedly, but because of the management's tough attitude, there has been no practical solution so far. Police officers negotiate. At the same time, they explained to the police station that the factory was indeed in the Chinese territory, and the police station should not interfere in labor disputes across the border. After the police station determined that the factory was indeed in the Chinese territory, it immediately withdrew a large number of Chinese and Western detectives.

Japan's Foreign Trade in the First Half of This Year

Imports exceed exports by 267 million yuan

The Japanese Commercial Counselor's Office in China received an official telegram from its home country yesterday stating that Japan's foreign trade in the first half of this year totaled 1,366,000,000 yuan, all calculated in Japanese yen. Exports accounted for 550,000,000 yuan, and imports accounted for 816,000,000 yuan. Exports decreased by 270,000,000 yuan compared with the same period last year. The main reasons are due to China's unprecedented vigorous boycott of Japanese goods, coupled with the global economic downturn, especially the decline of the American economy, as well as the high tariff barriers and import restrictions of most countries. Imports increased by 115,000,000 yuan compared with the same period last year. This is because people generally anticipate that domestic prices will rise after the gold is re-banned and import tariffs will be revised soon, so they have purchased foreign goods one after another. Due to these various reasons, Japan's foreign trade in the first half of the year resulted in an import surplus of 267,000,000 yuan, an increase of 150,000,000 yuan compared with the same period last year.

As for Japan's trade with China, the export value to China in May was 24,000,000 yuan, and the import value was 18,000,000 yuan, resulting in an export surplus of 600,000 yuan. From January to May, exports to China were only 98,000,000 yuan, resulting in an import surplus of 40,000 yuan. However, it was found that the value of Chinese goods exported to Japan in May decreased by 26% in Manchuria, 43% in northern China, 66% in central China, and 54% in southern China. Japanese goods exported to China increased by 50% in Manchuria and 26% in northern China, but decreased by 15% in central China and 70% in southern China.

Revitalizing industry. Our country has vast land and abundant resources, but the country is weak and the people are poor, and it is on the verge of bankruptcy. Abolishing Taels and Changing to Yuan: A Problem

The issue of abolishing taels and changing to yuan has been widely discussed recently. This is indeed a pressing issue for reforming China's monetary system, with significant implications for improving finance. Moreover, it directly affects all businesses and individuals nationwide. Recently, individuals have been conducting in-depth research on this issue and expressing their opinions daily. This newspaper, sparing no effort, has once again interviewed experts to gradually disclose any findings, aiming to elaborate further and provide references for those concerned about this issue.

Today's publication features the views of a certain gentleman in the financial sector. He has served in the financial industry for twenty years, known for his stable business management. Moreover, he dedicates his leisure time to research and has published works based on his experience, which have been praised by readers. He is indeed a businessman and scholar combined. Perhaps readers may also examine his views. The gentleman said:

The people of the nation have long hoped for the abolishment of taels and the adoption of yuan. Summarizing its benefits and simplicity, there are several points: (1) Merchants and private individuals only need to use one type of currency, the silver yuan, eliminating the need for two sets of accounts. (2) The financial industry also only needs to use one type of currency, the silver yuan, eliminating the need for two sets of accounts and two types of reserves. (3) Merchants who import using taels and sell using yuan often suffer losses due to the exchange rate differences between taels and yuan. Abolishing taels can eliminate this type of loss. (4) Various losses from conversion of silver taels and remittances between regions can be avoided. In the past ten years or so, abolishing taels and adopting yuan has become an inevitable trend. In the past, Shanghai mostly used taels as its standard. Qian Zhuang (money shops) used to only accept silver taels for deposits, but in recent years, qian zhuang have also started accepting silver yuan. Moreover, not only did the number of silver yuan deposits in banks suddenly exceed silver tael deposits, but the silver yuan deposits in qian zhuang also exceeded silver tael deposits. Recently, due to the abundance of silver yuan, the exchange rate for foreign silver dollars (yangli) has fallen to six qian and eight fen. Now is truly an excellent opportunity to abolish taels and adopt yuan.

Speaking of the motivation and history behind abolishing taels and adopting yuan, it can be traced back to around 1914 or 1915. At that time, the people of the nation were already enthusiastic about the need to unify the monetary system, especially because foreign banks had great power at the time, issuing a large number of currencies, causing monetary chaos, which was criticized by the people of the nation. Foreign banks used the eagle dollar as their standard. After research, the people of the nation unanimously advocated that the national currency, the silver yuan, must be used as the standard first. Only by first using the national currency, the silver yuan, as the standard, can it be gradually promoted inland, allowing the various silver taels in different regions to transition from complexity to unification, facilitating commerce and benefiting finance. Subsequently, the government implemented the National Currency Regulations, and the circulation of Yuan Shikai's silver dollar (Yuanbi) became increasingly widespread. However, because Yuanbi was low in value and eagle dollars were high, a unified currency system was yet to be achieved. During the May Fourth Movement in 1919, disturbances in various regions affected finance. The exchange rate for foreign silver dollars (yangli) in Shanghai rose to eight qian, causing public outrage. The investigation revealed that the amount of eagle dollars held by Chinese and foreign merchants was very small. Therefore, through the efforts of the Bankers' Association and Qianye Gonghui (Money Trade Association), it was agreed to abolish the market price of eagle dollars. Market circulation would only recognize one market price for the national currency, Yuanbi... The currency market price began to be unified. (According to this reporter, foreign banks, even the largest ones on the Bund, held very few eagle dollars, far less than the amount they had issued as reserves. Therefore, at that time, they could only nod in agreement. Song Hanzhang contributed the most effort in liaising with them.) From then until 1927, the Nationalist government was established. The government started minting Sun Yat-sen's silver dollar (Sunbi), and its circulation became increasingly widespread. Yuanbi also decreased. Naturally, Sunbi became the national currency. Now, the number of silver taels stored in Shanghai is decreasing day by day, while the number of silver yuan is increasing. As a result, the exchange rate for foreign silver dollars (yangli) has fallen to six qian and eight fen. (According to this reporter, the reason why there are so many silver yuan stored in Shanghai is that the interior of the country is unstable due to bandits and unrest, so cash has been concentrated in Shanghai. The desolation of the interior can be seen from this.) As a result, the amount of silver yuan melted down in Shanghai every day to make silver ingots is nearly three hundred thousand yuan. The silver melted still flows into foreign banks. At this time, there is an abundance of silver yuan and a shortage of silver taels. The opportunity to abolish taels and adopt yuan, which has been envisioned for more than ten years, has finally arrived.

Speaking of abolishing taels and adopting yuan, once the old system that has been used for a long time is abolished, doubts from some people are unavoidable. Here are a few points to alleviate the doubts:

(1) Customs duties: According to customs calculations, customs duties are calculated in Haiguan taels converted to silver yuan. After abolishing taels and adopting yuan, if the silver yuan amount is compared, and if one Haiguan tael is equivalent to 1.591 silver yuan (according to Zhang Naiyan's assumption of one silver yuan equivalent to seven qian of a regulation silver yuan), the difference is about 3%, which means customs revenue can be increased by 3%. Based on last year's total customs revenue, an additional six million one hundred thousand yuan can be obtained. Based on this extrapolation, even if the future conversion rate is one silver yuan equivalent to 7.05 or 7.06 or 7.1 qian of a regulation silver yuan, customs revenue can still be increased and will not be insufficient.

(2) Foreign exchange: For foreign exchange, as long as an official price is set, in the future, after abolishing taels, it can still be calculated using a fixed exchange rate. For example, if one regulation silver yuan tael is equivalent to a certain number of shillings and pence, in the future, one shilling will be equivalent to a certain number of silver yuan. Calculating silver yuan directly with foreign currency has absolutely no connection to anything else.

(3) Domestic remittance: In fact, silver is not used in various parts of China. Although there are differences between silver taels in different regions, they are all converted into Shanghai regulation silver yuan... Shanghai statutory silver taels are the standard. For example, Suzhou Bao silver and Hankou foreign example silver must also be converted into Shanghai regulation silver yuan in Shanghai. Because there is no silver stored inland, and it is converted into Shanghai regulation silver yuan, then after Shanghai abolishes taels and adopts yuan, it can be directly combined with the national currency. Following Shanghai in using silver yuan will be even more convenient.

(4) Debt and credit: The conversion rate for abolishing taels and adopting yuan has not yet been finalized. It may be 7.05 qian, or 7.06 qian, or 7.1 qian. However, on the day the decision is implemented (according to this reporter, the soonest is August 1st, and the latest is September 1st, but it has not yet been decided), debts and credits will be calculated at that day's rate. When merchants convert silver taels owed to them or to the silver and money shops into silver yuan, it may seem like there will be a loss. However, the silver and money shops must also convert the silver taels deposited by depositors into silver yuan and repay them. The silver and money shops have a lot of silver tael deposits. Therefore, the difference between the conversion of silver taels owed by merchants is not much. The silver and money shops will have no remaining profit to take advantage of.

(5) National currency: Currently, the responsibility for minting coins should be centralized at the Shanghai Mint. When minting coins, it must be absolutely transparent. Central and Western expert technicians should test the fineness. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Bankers' Association, Qianye Gonghui, and even the Foreign Bankers' Association can all supervise. If the results of the testing are announced at any time, then the fineness of the national currency will be excellent, and circulation will be no problem. Currently, the Hangzhou Mint has stopped minting coins, and the Nanjing Mint has no inventory. The Shanghai Mint, under the supervision of the Chinese people, should be able to happily fulfill the task of minting coins. (According to this reporter, there are still one or two mints inland, such as the Anhui coin and Sichuan coin, etc., whose fineness may be insufficient from time to time. Then the government should strictly prohibit the minting of low-quality national coins. If the government cannot prohibit it in a short period of time, then when these types of national coins flow to Shanghai, the Shanghai Mint should test them at any time. Those that do not meet the fineness standards should be prohibited from use and not accepted as a way to resist them. Then these inferior coins will naturally not be able to circulate. This requires the collective effort of the government and the business community.) Moreover, the Shanghai Mint has decided on a free minting policy, stipulating a legal price... Based on the amount of pure silver contained in today's silver yuan, plus the minting fee... In the future, when the financial community needs cash, it can entrust the mint to manufacture at any time. (According to this reporter, the amount of pure silver has a statutory rate, but the minting fee should absolutely not be high. Unifying the monetary system is a major national policy. When the government promotes it, it should not have a profit-seeking mentality and should even add a small subsidy from the national treasury to complete its mission.) (6) Paper currency: After abolishing taels, there is a concern that there may not be enough silver yuan in circulation, so paper currency must be used, leading to doubts about the issuance of paper currency. In fact, paper currencies issued now, such as the Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Zhongnan Bank, and Xingye Bank, have all gone through the procedures of inspection and public announcement by the Kai Jian Cha Gong Gao Ju. As for other banks that have not issued currency, the government will no longer grant them the right to issue currency. Therefore, the circulation of paper currency now is very different from the situation before 1927. Before 1927, there was no inspection, so there was a risk of excessive issuance. Now that the silver and money shops have publicly inspected, and the reserves are accurate, there is no possibility of excessive issuance of paper currency, and credit can be maintained. There will be no accidents.

Liang Jingwu Detained by Japanese Troops

Now Released from the Navy and Returns to Hong Kong

When the 19th Route Army was fighting in Shanghai, Liang Jingwu, the captain of the mine-laying team under Chen Ce of the Guangdong Fleet, volunteered to come to Shanghai with the mine-laying team members and joined the headquarters of the 19th Route Army, willing to assist in the Anti-Japanese War. After arriving in Shanghai, they set off to the Jiangyin area to lay mines to prevent Japanese warships from invading. After completing the work, they returned to Shanghai and resided in the Dongya Hotel. At that time, a car was parked outside the hotel gate. Liang went out, got into the car, and went with it. After Liang went missing, the headquarters of the 19th Route Army and Liang's friends searched everywhere, but there was no whereabouts. However, after Liang was detained by the Japanese, a friend of Liang's was also guarded by the Japanese army. At that time, the office immediately sent someone to report to Mayor Wu of the Municipal Government and asked him to negotiate with the Japanese side. After several exchanges, he was finally released. Currently, Mr. Liang has returned to Hong Kong a few days ago. The traitors who act as accomplices are really infuriating.

Local News Two

The Zhongwei Rental Ship Lawsuit

Hearing to Begin Tomorrow Morning

Chen Shuntong, manager of the Zhongwei Steamship Company, rented the company's Taiping ship to Yu'an Company in December of last year for a monthly rent of 13,500 yuan. There was a contract stating that if war broke out between China and a foreign country and affected the operation, both parties could unconditionally terminate the contract and settle the accounts. When the Sino-Japanese War began, Zhao Yuntai, the manager of Yu'an, suddenly thought that he had encountered the facts within the contract, so he negotiated with Chen to terminate the contract. However, Zhongwei believed that since both parties had not formally declared war in the Anti-Japanese War, it still did not constitute a war act in legal terms, so they refused to terminate the lease. Yu'an then hired three lawyers, Yang Hanzhi, Zhang Jiahui, and Ye Shaoying, to sue Zhongwei and Chen Shuntong in the First Special District Court, requesting a judgment to order the return of all prepaid funds. Zhongwei received the court's notice and also hired a lawyer to file a statement of defense and filed a counterclaim. It is now known that the case has been assigned to Judge Yang Peng by the court. Judge Yang has scheduled a special hearing in the Ninth Tribunal on the morning of the 14th of this month (i.e., tomorrow). At that time, the plaintiff and defendant lawyers will have a fierce debate on whether the January 28 Incident constitutes a war.

Continued Hearing of the Cao Akun Assassination Case

Cao Akun, a native of Jiangyin residing at No. 50 Renji Road, Pudong, was shot and killed on the morning of the 22nd of last month at 5:00 a.m. in the assembly hall opened by Ningbo native Sang Dingsheng on the fourth floor of Heliyuan at No. 78 Minguo Road, French Concession, while playing mahjong. On the morning of the same day at 10:00 a.m., detectives from the special agency of the French Concession police arrested a related person, Xu Changyu, in Pudong and sent him to the Second Special District Court for interrogation and investigation. The details have been recorded in previous reports. The police found that Xu was indeed involved and was the lookout at the scene. Yesterday morning, Judge Li Changnian sat in the Criminal First Tribunal to continue the trial. First, Gu Shouxi, the police lawyer, stated the case, saying that the police had investigated and found that the defendant was indeed suspected of murder and was being prosecuted under Article 288 of the Criminal Law for premeditated murder. If the court finds other circumstances, the police can change the articles at any time. Under questioning, the defendant Xu Changyu confessed that he was 22 years old, a native of Ningbo, residing at No. 36 Changxing Lane, Dongchang Road, Pudong, currently unemployed, and acquainted with the fugitive Tang Yuanqing, also known as "Little Taizhou", "Little Dog", "Little Xi", "Wang Wang Jiao", and "A Hu". At 5:00 p.m. on June 27, he met "Little Xi" on the road, who invited him to Room 35 of the Central Hotel in Xiaodongmen, where he saw a Mr. Ma and "Little Taizhou", "Little Dog", "A Hu", etc. "Little Xi" said that they had robbed 4,000 yuan of opium with Cao Akun, but Cao had swallowed it all up, so they wanted to kill him and ordered me to keep track of Cao's whereabouts. Later, I, Lu Aliu, found out that Cao was playing mahjong on the floor of Heliyuan. That night, everyone brought guns and went to wait. Until 5:00 a.m. the next day, Mr. Ma ordered me, "Wang Wang Jiao", "A Hu", and "Little Taizhou" to be the lookout, and Mr. Ma and "Little Dog" went upstairs and shot Cao dead. I was arrested at 10:00 a.m. that day, etc. Cao Dai, the wife of the deceased, reported that there was still a wanted criminal, the defendant's father, Zhou Baoxiang, also known as "Little Baoxiang", who was arrested by the Public Security Bureau after a woman reported the crime in Pudong. She requested that the case be brought up for interrogation. Also, Cao Ziqi, the deceased's cousin, arrived at the case and testified to the deceased's last words. The court verified the confession and ordered the hearing to be adjourned to the 18th, with additional witnesses to be summoned for questioning. The defendant was returned to custody.

Chen Jianchu's Wife Sues Him for Abandonment

Chen Jianchu, a Cantonese, runs the Nanshengliang Confectionery and Keming Photo Studio in Shanghai. He currently lives with his two concubines, Chen Daxi and Tan Aping, at No. 293 Renzhi Lane, North Sichuan Road. His wife, Chen Lianglianyou, lives elsewhere with her adopted daughter, Yuying. After the trial, the court found that the plaintiff's reasons were insufficient and dismissed the case. As for alimony, she was instructed to file a separate lawsuit in the civil court. She has now hired lawyer Xi Yafu to sue Chen for alimony, requesting a judgment ordering the defendant to pay alimony of 5,995 yuan. She said that she married the defendant at the age of 19 and has been with him for 16 years, helping him greatly with his career. The defendant was originally destitute. Her private savings of more than 2,000 yuan were all spent. After the defendant became rich, he disliked her aging and took many concubines, listening to their words and treating her like a thorn in his side, repeatedly trying to trick her into leaving. When the January 28 Incident occurred, the defendant only took his two concubines and fled, leaving her and her daughter behind. After the incident was over, he did not allow her to return home. This is malicious abandonment, so she filed a lawsuit, requesting a judgment ordering the defendant to pay her living expenses to avoid starvation. Yesterday morning, Judge Shen of the First Special District Court opened the trial. The defendant did not appear. According to the plaintiff's lawyer, the defendant Chen Jianchu is wealthy and intentionally ignores the plaintiff's life. He was caught selling opium privately by the police, and both concubines were arrested. Later, Chen generously requested 6,000 gold coins to bail them out. His attitude of favoring concubines and suppressing his wife can be seen. Now he avoids appearing in court, which is even more contemptuous of the court. Judge Shen then interrogated Chen Lianglianyou and ordered her to go out and try to reconcile. The hearing was adjourned for further verification.

Private Dismantling of Li Jishen's Radio Case

Each Offender Receives Separate Sentence

Local youth Zhang Zijie, on the afternoon of the 14th of last month, along with Huang Axiang, Huang Minggao, Zhao Fugui, and Ping Ade, five in total, hired a car and trespassed into the residence of Li Jishen, the current Central Committee member, located at No. 163, Route Luber, French Concession. They dismantled a wireless radio without permission and hid it in the Xitusuo area of the Jessfield Road. That night, detectives from the French Concession's special agency apprehended Zhang and the other four at the Eastern Hotel, recovered the stolen goods, and handed them over to the Second Special District Court. Zhang confessed to having been instructed by Chen Guisheng to dismantle the radio and hired lawyer Wang Shizong to defend him. Huang and the others confessed that they were invited by Zhang. The trial has concluded and a sentence date set. Yesterday was the sentencing date. At 9:30 AM, Judge Li Changnian ascended the bench in the Criminal Division and sentenced Zhang Zijie, Huang Axiang, Huang Minggao, and Zhao Fugui to six months of imprisonment for privately dismantling the property of others. Ping Ade, due to having committed crimes in both the British and French concessions, was sentenced to eight months of imprisonment. The number of days detained before the verdict will be deducted from the prison sentence at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment.
