A Dead Body in a Bedroll

Abandoned Beside a Sugarcane Stall

Lin Zhengfang, a 47-year-old man from Xinghua, runs a fruit stall at Datong Wharf in Nanshi. Yesterday, around 1:00 AM, Lin was selling sugarcane at the wharf as the Zhida steamer, docked there, was preparing to set sail. Suddenly, a man wearing a white cloth short shirt and pants, carrying a bedroll wrapped in a straw mat, paid Lin eight copper coins for a stalk of sugarcane. He then said to Lin, "Friend, please watch this bedroll for me. I'm going to buy a pack of cigarettes and will be right back." Lin agreed. Unexpectedly, the man never returned. When the Zhida steamer set sail, Lin reported the matter to Lu Wenji, the guard on duty at the 35th post. Officer Lu, upon hearing the report, came and opened the straw mat-wrapped bedroll. Inside, there was cotton padding. When the cotton padding was unwrapped, a corpse was revealed, belonging to a male, about fifty years old. The deceased was wearing a white cloth short shirt, a gray silk-lined jacket, black satin cotton pants, and white cotton socks. Greatly alarmed, he immediately reported the situation to the First District Headquarters. The District Head, considering the matter a case of homicide, ordered Lu Yongde, the local head of the 16th Pupu, to report it to the Shanghai Local Court for an inquest.

Daughter-in-Law Hangs Herself After Discord with Mother-in-Law

Liu Zuyin, a 24-year-old man from Ningbo, works as a steward on the Yongxing steamer of the Ning Shao Shipping Company. Due to the Yongxing being temporarily suspended by the government, Liu is currently in Shanghai, residing at No. 972, Yile Lane, Tangshan Road. His wife, Mei Qing, also from Ningbo, is 20 years old and works as a factory girl at the Minsheng Tobacco Company, earning over ten yuan a month to supplement the family income. Liu's mother is still alive and also goes out to work as a maid, saving expenses. However, the mother-in-law and daughter-in-law have conflicting opinions and have always been at odds. Last year, Liu's father passed away, leaving behind a mountain of debt. Liu's mother pawned her daughter-in-law Mei Qing's clothes for money and also ordered her to work hard, leading to frequent quarrels between the two. Yesterday evening, Mei Qing suddenly had a desire to end her life, falsely claiming she was going to take a bath. She locked herself in the bathroom for an hour. Her husband became suspicious and broke down the door, only to find his wife had hanged herself on the bed. She had already died.

Playing with a Shell Causes Disaster

Four Fingers Blown Off, One Eye Blinded

At No. 299, Taixing Road, Wusong, there is a garden, which is the villa of former Chamber of Commerce President Gu Dan's nest. Gu has a nephew named Mingwei, who is 18 years old and a student at a university in Shanghai. He is currently on vacation at home. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, Mingwei was walking in the garden when he happened to pick up the nose of an anti-aircraft shell. He returned home and repeatedly played with it, unaware that it contained a powerful explosive. Unexpectedly, upon hitting the ground, it suddenly exploded, shaking the house. Mr. Gu and his family, hearing the noise, were shocked to see Mingwei lying in a pool of blood, unconscious. They quickly hired a car and sent him to the Fumin Hospital in this city for treatment. It is said that four fingers on his left hand were blown off, and his left eye has been blinded. However, there is no immediate danger to his life.

Old Man Commits Suicide by Drowning

Xu Renbao, also known as Zhilin, from Chuansha, residing at No. 10, Lane 43, Old Street, Xujiahui Town, Shanghai, was 61 years old. His first wife had passed away twenty years ago, and he married a fellow villager, Ms. Shen, as his second wife. They have seven sons and two daughters. The eldest son, Yongqing, works at the Shijiazhuang Zhengtai Railway Administration. The second and youngest sons are currently studying at school, and the youngest is still in diapers. Although Xu is over sixty, he is still vigorous and works as an accountant at the Tongmao Beef Restaurant on Jing'an Temple Road, leaving early and returning late, as he has always done for ten years. Recently, due to his children's quarrels at home, Renbao scolded them, leading to a disagreement with Ms. Shen. Stimulated by this, Renbao suddenly had a desire to end his life. The day before yesterday morning at 6:00 AM, he went to the restaurant wearing old clothes and did some tidying up. At 11:00 AM, he left the restaurant. His colleagues, seeing his attire and his sorrowful face, were very surprised and asked him where he was going. He replied that he was going shopping and would return soon, so they did not suspect anything. Unexpectedly, Xu left and committed suicide by drowning. In the afternoon, his colleagues did not see Xu return to the restaurant, so they notified Xu's family and asked people to search everywhere, but there was no trace of him. They then submitted Xu's photo to the Water Police and the Lifesaving Bureau for searching, but there was still no sign of him. Until yesterday afternoon, Xu's body was found on the surface of the Huangpu River at Lujiazui. The Lifesaving Bureau managed to retrieve it and notified the family to identify it. It was confirmed to be him. That night, Xu's wife prepared a coffin and had him buried.

Vagrant Commits Suicide Due to Poverty

Shao Fangge, a 25-year-old man from Gaoyou, Jiangbei, did not engage in honest work and had a habit of wandering around the Linping Road area of Hongkou. Due to unbearable poverty, he sneaked into the iron gate of Renpin Lane, Linping Road, the night before last and hanged himself. He was discovered yesterday, and the Fifth District Third Precinct was notified. The local head, Li A'er, reported it to the Local Court for an inquest. The body was then collected by a charitable organization.

Boat Girl Commits Suicide by Poison

Liu Jinxiang, a 20-year-old woman from Ningbo, was quite beautiful. Her home was at No. 1255, Xinji Bank Road. Her father worked as a boatman, but the family income was not enough to make ends meet. Recently, Jinxiang quarreled with her father over the issue of moving houses due to the cramped living space. Unable to vent her resentment, she became weary of life and secretly took opium to kill herself. Her mother, Zhu, noticed and rushed her to Renji Hospital. However, due to severe poisoning, she soon died. The hospital notified the police station, who sent detectives to investigate. The corpse was transported to the forensic examination office on Fellen Road. Yesterday morning, Guo Wei, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, arrived at the office to conduct an examination. After questioning the family members of the deceased, he determined that the deceased was a female who had died of opium poisoning. The body was handed over to her mother, Liu Zhu, to collect and bury with a signed statement.

Pudong Zhenxiu Prepares Alumni Association

The Shanghai Municipal Zhenxiu Elementary School in Yangjiadu, Pudong, formerly the Second High Elementary School of Shanghai County, was established in the late Qing Dynasty, almost thirty years ago. A preparation office was set up at the school. After several preparation meetings, various investigations, receptions, and the drafting of regulations are nearing completion. The survey form has also been prepared, printed, and distributed.

Mr. Li Qicheng was a native of Qibao, learned and skilled in calligraphy. He currently held the position of clerk in the Shanghai South District Defense Corps. Foreman Falls to His Death

Zhang Xiangfa, a foreman at the Pan Rongji Construction Factory on Meizhou Road, was a native of Ningbo, 29 years old. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, he was inspecting at a height of about three zhang (approximately 10 meters) when he suddenly fell, breaking his head and dying on the spot.

Robbers Open Fire, Injuring People

At the straw shed on Qimei Road, Hujia Muqiao, around 9:30 PM last night, four robbers arrived, demanding money from door to door. The shed dwellers refused and shouted for help. The robbers fled, two of them holding pistols, firing shots along the way as a warning. Stray bullets hit Li Xiaohouzi and Liu Changlong. Li is a native of Jiangbei, 27 years old, and runs a tiger stove in Hujia Muqiao. He was passing through the area to collect money. Liu Changlong, 51 years old, is a native of Jiangbei and a road worker for the Public Works Department, living in the straw shed. He was eating dinner at the door when he was shot in the left waist by the robbers. His injury is relatively minor. Li Xiaohouzi was shot in the abdomen, and his condition is quite dangerous. Both are being treated at the Tongren Hospital.

Sentence for Illegally Manufacturing Opium Substitutes

Chief Detective Wang Changgen and Zhao Bingkun of the Public Concession General Inspectorate previously uncovered an illegal morphine manufacturing operation at No. 18 Jiaxing Road. They arrested the main suspect, a Japanese man named Nakamura (also known as Coco Ka), along with Chinese nationals Fang Yinbao, Su Ahui, Diao Jinsheng, and others. They seized a large quantity of morphine drugs and took them all to the Hongkou Police Station. The Japanese Coco Ka was handed over to the Japanese Consulate for handling, where he was fined 50 yuan. The others, Fang Yinbao, etc., were handed over to the First Special District Local Court for trial and sentenced to imprisonment. Subsequently, detectives handling the case obtained a related suspect, Ye Qingli, a native of Fujian, and handed him over to the Special Court for repeated interrogations, ordering him to be released on bail pending trial. This has been reported in the newspapers. Yesterday morning, Judge Fu Lin opened court to interrogate him. The police lawyer and the lawyer of the defendant Ye Qinghe debated for a long time. Judge Fu then announced the verdict in court: the defendant Ye Qinghe was sentenced to four years of imprisonment for the crime of jointly manufacturing opium substitutes, and fined 5,000 yuan. If he cannot pay, he will be imprisoned for one day for every three yuan, but not exceeding one year. The defendant's lawyer declared that he would appeal, and the court approved it. During the appeal period, he will remain on his original bail.

Hot Water Bottle Industry Asks All Circles to Identify Domestic Goods

The Hot Water Bottle Manufacturing Industry Association of this city yesterday issued a letter to citizens from all walks of life (excerpted above): A hot water bottle is a necessity for modern home and travel. Unfortunately, they all come from foreign countries, and enemy goods account for the majority. The huge loss of assets is a concern for those who know. In recent years, although Chinese people have manufactured them, they have not made concrete publicity, so domestic goods and enemy goods cannot be fully distinguished, allowing the rights and interests to flow out, like water flowing into a valley. Since the September 18th Incident, the heat of Chinese people's boycott of goods has reached a boiling point, and the sales of enemy goods have suddenly dried up. After the signing of the Shanghai War Agreement, Japanese merchants returned and secretly planned activities. There are even many unscrupulous merchants who are greedy for profit, risk being scolded, and pass off enemy goods as domestic products, deceiving the Chinese people. Their crimes are punishable, and their flesh is not enough to eat. Our association is a group of manufacturers of pure domestic hot water bottles, and it is our duty to run around and appeal. We hope that all patriotic compatriots will widely introduce them. In the future, domestic products will be popular and enemy goods will disappear. Everything depends on the care and promotion of all circles. As for manufacturing technology, we strive for excellence. We hope that people from all walks of life will not change their original intention of saving the country and carefully identify them.

Four Banks Issue Preparation Report

132nd

The Four Banks Reserve is jointly established by Yanye, Jincheng, Zhongnan, and Dalu banks to handle the issuance of Zhongnan Bank banknotes. According to the library’s regulations, enough banknotes are issued. At least 60% of the cash must be prepared, and at most 40% of the guarantee must be prepared. An announcement is made once a week, and the auditors and accountants of the four banks examine it. The following is a transcript of the 132nd announcement of the Shanghai Preparation Library on July 9, 21st year. The amount of banknotes in circulation is 18,623,257 yuan. The total amount of the reserve is 18,623,257 yuan, including 11,449,526 yuan and 87 cents of cash reserve and 7,173,730 yuan and 13 cents of guarantee reserve.

Central Bank Inspection Report

130th Time

The 130th Inspection Report on the Issuance Preparation of the Central Bank states: This association is responsible for inspecting the reserve funds for the issuance of exchange coupons of the bank in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations. On July 11, 21st year of the Republic of China, Supervisor Wang Yihou conducted the 130th inspection at the bank's Issuance Bureau. The results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) The total amount of exchange coupons issued is 2,981,7997 yuan, including 2,693,1803 silver yuan coupons and 2,886,194 legal currency coupons. The total amount of exchange coupon reserves is 2,981,7997 yuan, including 2,452,3997 silver yuan in cash reserves. The cash reserve is stored in the bank’s issuing treasury, 2,190,05,832 yuan and 74 cents, stored in branches in various ports, 1,466,171 yuan, and stored in counterparties, 1,151,993 yuan and 26 cents. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 5,294,000 silver yuan. (B) The total amount of customs gold exchange coupons issued is 377,089 yuan and 40 cents. The total amount of customs gold exchange coupon reserves is 377,089 yuan and 40 cents. The preparations include 4,201 taels, 4 mace, and 9 fen of standard gold, which are stored in the bank's issuing treasury at a fixed price of 60, equivalent to 252,089 yuan and 40 cents in customs gold, and 50,000 US dollars are stored in counterparties in this port at a fixed price of 40, equivalent to 125,000 yuan in customs gold. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank Exchange Coupon Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The inspection result shows that the cash exceeds 60% and the guarantee is less than 40%, which is in line with the regulations. This report is hereby made. July 11, 21st year of the Republic of China, Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank.

Jiangsu Stamp Tax Bureau for Tobacco and Alcohol

Director Zhang Receives Commendation

It was reported yesterday that Director Zhang Yizhi of the Jiangsu Stamp Tax Bureau for Tobacco and Alcohol received a special order from the Ministry of Finance, which stated: "According to the case presented by the Stamp Tax Office for Tobacco and Alcohol, although many provincial stamp tax bureaus for tobacco and alcohol have been able to remit the full amount of tax revenue to the treasury each month, or even exceed the quota, there are also not a few who use various excuses to remit short amounts or delay payment. Without distinguishing between rewards and punishments, it would be insufficient to encourage them. The Jiangsu Stamp Tax Bureau for Tobacco and Alcohol has been able to remit the full amount of tax revenue in May and June, and even exceed the quota. Therefore, it should be commended." The order also stated: "The sufficiency of the treasury depends on the efforts of the provincial tax bureaus. The director of the bureau is concerned about the national economy and has made every effort to collect taxes, which is commendable. It is hoped that he will continue to work hard to collect taxes and remit them regularly, so as to enrich tax revenue. We have high expectations."

Special Feature

When Will the Abolition of Taels and Adoption of Yuan Take Place? (3)

Jiang Lizhao

Of course, we cannot confuse the entire inventory with the cash reserve of banknotes. Then, where are the silver deposits and the silver reserve for private bank notes? According to a report by Mr. Faithfull, the former chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Council, the number of private bank notes issued by Shanghai money shops and circulating on the market each year is about 200 million taels or more. In Shanghai, which uses silver as its standard, the total amount of trade and deposits is unknown and impossible to calculate. However, its cash reserve, including foreign coins, is only more than 53 million taels, and at most only more than 95 million taels. Is this a paper head or a real head? The money industry issues private bank notes based on the excellent transfer system and unlimited liability credit, and people do not doubt it. Is there a danger of issuing unreserved banknotes after the abolition of taels and the adoption of yuan? It is just a system. The real head and paper head are not worth worrying about. (4) The issue of recording units and the interest of one mill, two mils, and five mils is definitely not the real reason why the money industry opposes the abolition of taels and the adoption of yuan. Changing the accounting unit is just a matter of a hand's turn. The compromise market price is set by the day, and what can be done elsewhere without hindrance, is Shanghai any different? As for the interest of one mill, two mils, and five mils, it has the suspicion of exploitation and should be abolished. Commercial banks in various countries also charge handling fees for commercial transactions. It seems that a fixed handling fee can be charged to compensate for the loss after the abolition of taels. Merchants all avoid harm and seek profit. The money shop business is stable and agile, and it must have its own value of existence. It is determined that it depends on silver for maintenance, so it can be trusted widely and for a long time. Otherwise, if there is exploitation of one mill, two mils, and five mils, why would merchants be happy to deal with them? Therefore, after the abolition of taels, if it is replaced by handling fees, the money industry will still not suffer any loss. If it can be abolished and exempted, then the exploitation is gone, and it will be easier to attract customers. People are the same, and their hearts are the same. The development of business will be even better than it is now, which can be predicted.

The above are still reasons of the past. Since the Shanghai Incident, the foreign bottom in Shanghai and Tianjin has been thicker than ever before. There is a proposal in Tianjin to organize a public treasury to eliminate foreign dollars and finance funds. The Shanghai Lehi has fallen to 6 cents and 8 mils. The reason is that there is little production in the rural areas of the interior, and the use of foreign dollars has suddenly decreased. All the necessities of life depend on foreign goods, which must be purchased with silver. Silver and foreign dollars cannot be used interchangeably. Therefore, the supply of foreign dollars exceeds demand, and the demand for silver exceeds supply. Silver dollars are originally daily currency, but they are useless. There is a saying that looking at white rice makes you hungry. This is what it means. The country is in such a difficult situation, and we still do not plan to alleviate the unnecessary urgency of the financial community. What is the intention?

Since the principle is clear, let us now talk about the method. 1. The government, the financial industry, and the Chamber of Commerce should immediately form a committee to implement the abolition of taels and the adoption of yuan, negotiate the equivalent value of silver in new and old contracts and the existing standard silver ingots in foreign dollars, and the date of implementation, and submit it to the government for promulgation and mandatory implementation. The foreign dollar market in various places will be closed from the date of implementation. 2. Customs duties and land taxes will be collected in silver dollars. The market price of international exchange will be calculated in silver dollars. Domestic exchange rates will be limited to transportation points. 3. Instruments denominated in silver will be prohibited from circulation. Newly incurred silver debts will not be accepted by courts at all levels. 4. The Central Mint should start minting as soon as possible and implement free minting. The original mints in various places must be under its jurisdiction or even closed down to avoid discrepancies and return to unity. A chemical inspection committee will be attached to the mint, which will be jointly formed by the government, the financial industry, and the Chamber of Commerce, and the chemical inspection will be made public. The machines of the factory have arrived early, and the scale is the first in the world. Every 24 hours, it can mint 1 million coins. Shanghai needs 500,000 to 600,000 coins a day, which, combined with the Ninghang factories, is enough to supply the whole country. If it can be implemented, then the credit and supply of silver dollars will be flawless. 5. Provinces and ports must not have local orders prohibiting the export of silver dollars to facilitate their flow. 6. The Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications should cooperate fully with the mint to fully supply the need for silver dollars. 7. From the date of implementation, financial institutions shall not accept silver deposits, nor shall they make silver loans. The bookkeeping of all industries must be in silver dollars. Violators will be fined. 8. After implementation, if it is discovered that there are still Chinese people depositing silver in foreign banks, if there is evidence, they will be severely punished, and the governments should notify the embassies and consulates of various countries to take note of this when implementing it. 9. The original furnace masters, shop assistants, and craftsmen should be sent to the mint for registration and employment, and assigned according to their talents to avoid unemployment. The above methods, the first four items are mostly the original suggestions of Mr. Jin Guobao, and the author has only slightly supplemented them. I hereby declare to avoid the suspicion of plagiarism. I deeply hope that the government and society will implement them as soon as possible. Then, the first step in organizing the currency system will be successful, and there will be a lot of convenience in the financial and fiscal affairs during the national crisis. (End)

Correspondence

Declaration of the Chinese People's Civil Rights Promotion Association

Ma Xiangbo

(Attached) Summary of the Constitution

1. On the People The people have (natural human rights), that is, the right to freedom of body, the right to property, the right to residence, the right to business, the right to freedom of thought, the right to freedom of speech, publication, assembly, etc., the right to practice (religions that do not harm people), men between the ages of eighteen and forty have the obligation to serve in the military, and after the age of eighteen, or after graduating from middle school, have the obligation to practice military exercises for one year, and women after the age of eighteen have the obligation to practice nursing and repairing military weapons.

Nine out of ten people are producers, and one out of ten is a guide to production. In terms of analysis, nine out of ten are farmers, herdsmen, watermen, firemen, artisans, and foresters, and one out of ten are professionals and public officials. Accordingly, people should receive vocational education and training. Each county should set up schools for farming, animal husbandry, industry, forestry, etc., each county should set up a middle school, and each united prefecture should set up a university.

The people have the right to vote and the right to be elected, but first they should elect local elders as representatives, and appoint two or three young people with professional qualifications as secretaries to the representatives, and have the right to audit and discuss with the representatives of the same prefecture whether the representatives should be approved or rejected. The number of elected representatives in each place is not fixed, so as to avoid the accumulation of bribery and electoral corruption in the election. (The American election is a waste of money. Belgium changed from a republic to a constitutional monarchy, and some say it was to avoid the burden of re-election every three to five years.) As for those who attend the National People's Congress, the number of attendees is limited by drawing lots to avoid endless discussions. Their travel expenses are borne by the state, and their attendance allowance is borne by the local area.

Those who are incompetent can be replaced by drawing lots.

2. On Politics The president and ministers must be nationals, have received education above secondary school, and have more than fifteen years of experience in the national society after the age of twenty, and have no criminal record or bad deeds such as financial, sexual, or treasonous conspiracies before being eligible for election. The officials who are close to the people are also the same. Each uses people from this county and prefecture, or people who are registered or honorary registered. All agency officials must have scientific knowledge if they have full-time duties, and they must be recruited by the agency's scientific examination method, learn the archives of this department, and learn the situation of the states and prefectures for three years before they can receive official salaries and be promoted based on their qualifications. They cannot be removed or demoted without fault. They can retire after one year of service, and still receive half their salary. They can retire according to regulations after the age of sixty. All salaries are accounted for independently, using bank checks and individual receipts to eliminate corruption. They cannot wage war or recruit soldiers without the consent of the people, and those who violate this will be severely punished. All actions and departures have special officials, and they are not allowed to borrow civilian houses, boats, or vehicles, and they are not allowed to use military tickets or forcibly conscript laborers, etc. (To be continued)

Free Talk

Research on Amber and Mustard Seeds

Ma Xiangbo, Ninety-Three-Year-Old Man

Since the publication of the "Original Object" in June 11th, Mr. Cao Zhongyuan first inquired about the origin of "Amber and Mustard Seeds," which was published on June 16th. Then, Mr. Tao Zaidong and Li Mo submitted articles, which have also been published one after another. Now, Mr. Cao Zhongyuan's letter proves that "Amber" is a transliteration and has meaning, so it is specially published. Old Xiang also talked to the reporter about the fact that many gems are from foreign countries, which coincides with what Mr. Cao said. In addition, please send any discussion documents on this issue to Mr. Cao at the Dahua Wireless Electric Company Factory, No. 48-50 Wenlin Road, Shanghai. Han Zhi

The story of amber and mustard seeds. Old Man of Ninety-Three and Mr. Tao Zaidong and Li Zhu have all written a lot of quotations. scattered in this journal. Hong Bo is admirable. However, there are still doubts. Mr. Li quoted Guo Pu's Shantujing Tuzan. The meaning of the text is slightly different from the English translation. If I have already inquired about it from an Englishman. It is not a mistranslation. That is, there is another basis. Lei Zue of the Song Dynasty said, "Amber is like blood. If you rub it with a cloth and heat it, the real one will attract mustard seeds." Li Shizhen must identify it as grass and not mustard seeds. I don't know that amber is heated and rubbed. Everything that is light, dry, thin and small can be absorbed, so Ji Wanlin Yun said, "Amber is heated on the skin. Use a little piece of paper. Keep it an inch away. It will naturally fly up." Lu Fannian was only twelve years old. The talk of crooked needles and rotten mustard is not a true knower of physics. Clouds do not follow earth dragons, and winds do not follow earth tigers. Wang Chong then said that fake dunmou cannot take mustard, and fake magnets cannot attract needles. From the point of view of today's physical experiments, the words of the ancients are all seemingly true but actually false. Examining the book DeAnima by the great Greek philosopher Aristotle, it has been found that amber is a mysterious thing. It is said that its function is the same as that of a magnet. When Aristotle was born. In our country, it was before the Shang Dynasty Wuding. The era was very early. Later, Greek and Roman writers such as Pliny and Thales (one of the seven great Greek thinkers) all have the same records. Calculate the age. Long before Confucius was born. The ancient Persian name for amber was Kuhruba. The meaning is to pick up grass and mustard. The name of magnet is AhangRuba, which means to attract iron. It can be seen that the two things have the same function but different properties. It was discovered early at that time. One is static electricity, the other is magnetism. The properties are different. Not suitable for mixing. What the ancients did not know. It was not until Dr. Gilbert came out in 1600 AD. The name Electricity was first used. It is transformed from the Greek word Hlektron. The meaning is only to explain amber. However, it was late in the season of Emperor Shenzong of the Ming Dynasty in our country. This is the merit of Westerners' creation. Yu explores the allusions. Contains two meanings. One is as Mr. Li pointed out. The second is when and who got this invention by the friction method. If this meaning is not clear, the confusion will not be resolved. After the Ming Dynasty, electricity was referred to as magnetism. The sight of Zhongxi Longdong. For thousands of years. It belongs to another matter again. The scientific deeds of our country. Records are often brief. Like a tree being drilled with grass. History books always end with three or five words. It is speculated that the story of picking up mustard seeds may not be in the Shang and Zhou dynasties. It was destroyed in the Qin Fire. As a result, there is no way to investigate it. The old things quoted in the previous paragraph of this article are all works after the Tang and Song dynasties. Where does its origin come from? Those who can tell its details. Please teach me.

Casual Notes from Hangzhou

— Zhi Zheng

Mr. Zheng Yangsheng, director of the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Transportation Office, went to Hangzhou on official business to inspect road affairs. The reporter accompanied him. He spent a day and a half in Hangzhou. In addition to studying road construction and reform, he also saw and heard many other things worth recording. Therefore, I will describe one or two to leave a trace.

The False National Narrative of the Northeast Returnee In the car, he met a certain gentleman who had just returned from the Northeast. According to the conversation, the situation in the false country was quite funny. Puyi is called the head of state, but in fact he is like a prisoner. No one is allowed to see him without the consent of the Japanese. Chonghou, the former treasurer of Jilin, who was a relative of the royal family, once saw the emperor. The matter was detected by the Japanese and he was detained. Puyi's own bed is also equipped with a radio. Even the conversation between the couple can be heard clearly by the Japanese. His pain can be imagined. Zheng Xiaoxu is called the President of the Executive Yuan, but in fact he is like a puppet. Apart from entrusting his son as a secretary, he cannot directly appoint even a lower-level official. The power is purely in the hands of the Japanese advisers. Zheng's old age is like this, which is also regrettable. When the investigation team was about to arrive in the false country, a notice was suddenly posted one day, saying that a play would be performed somewhere. Not only were the audience not charged tickets, but they were also given two dimes and a steamed bun. The whole city was shocked and rushed to watch it. Who knew that after entering the theater, they were led by the hosts into a room and asked each person to sign their name, address, and occupation in a pre-prepared book. Then they were paid. At that time, they did not know what the intention was. Later, when the investigation team arrived in Shenyang, the Japanese handed over this book and said that all those who signed it had requested the investigation team to recognize the false country. There are many other similar funny stories. In addition, telegrams and letters are all checked. However, those letters and telegrams that they consider to have reactionary tendencies are not detained. They are delivered as usual. Those who receive the telegrams must declare the reasons to the police station within five days to avoid being prosecuted. Otherwise, once the deadline has passed, they will be imprisoned.

The Scorching Heat of Hangzhou After the car passed Jiaxing, the weather gradually became hotter. When we arrived in Hangzhou, it was unbearably hot. It was even worse at night. The lake water was boiling, which made people step back. The ancients said that Hangzhou is surrounded by mountains, like being at the bottom of a cauldron. It is true. In the evening, the colleagues at Hangzhou Station held a public banquet for the director at the railway dormitory, gathering together in an unprecedented grand occasion. Director Zheng gave a speech on the spot, detailing the handling of the January 28th Incident, and encouraging each other to cooperate and help each other. The next morning, the director went to inspect the Moganshan hostel, which was still being planned. I returned in advance, and said with a smile to the people who sent me off, "From now on, I will be free from the sea of heat." We all laughed together.

Yangmei

— Holding Buddha

When the plum rain is dripping from the eaves, the Yangmei is on the market again. The trees are beautiful, and the beads are like purple and black jade. We wander in the mountains, which is really mouth-watering. Tang Zhang Bi's poem says: "Yangmei is ripe in the tall forest with rain." This is a real situation. Therefore, although Yangmei is a temperate plant, it is suitable for hot and humid mountainous areas. Its nature is very similar to that of lychee, which is described as "One horse racing with red dust, and the concubine smiled." Our eastern Zhejiang is backed by mountains and faces the sea. The sea products are certainly rich. Bao Mingyuan said in his letter to his sister that there are all kinds of hog heads, elephant trunks, mang beards, needle tails, stone crabs, soil clams, swallows, and sparrow clams, and folded armor, curved teeth, reverse scales, and reversed tongues. There are also mountain products, such as Yangmei, which can be compared with loquat, lychee, and forest oranges. The Natural History says: "There is a chapter name in the land, then Yangmei will grow." For example, Cixi, anciently known as Gouzhang, so it produces a lot of Yangmei. Especially the Yangmei produced in the west, called "Bodhi Seed," has small cores and a sweet taste, and is especially famous. In addition, Shangyu in Zhejiang and Dongting in Jiangsu also produce Yangmei. There is also a kind of white Yangmei, which is lighter in color than the ordinary one and has a very sweet taste. It is said that there is Yangmei Wuwu in Hangzhou. There is an old woman named Jin in Wuwu. Because the Yangmei she grows is very good, "Yangmei Wuwu" and "Jin Po Yangmei" have become famous. Dongpo's Notes says: "There are hundreds of moon galleries in Fantian Temple, and there are many Yangmei in front of the court." What he said in his poem: "Dreaming around Wushan Queyue Gallery, Yangmei Lu oranges feel fragrant." refers to this matter.

There are many Yangmei poems: Dongpo also has a poem that says: "Zhu Chang in the south village and Lu in the north village, white flowers and green leaves do not wither in winter: Yangmei is an evergreen tree, growing in the mountains, and it blooms with yellow and white flowers in spring. Hanging red and purple in the misty rain, Shi Renlychee is a pioneer." Lu Fangweng said: "I have not loved the pile of fire jade, Yangmei is also called fire jade, also called fire fruit. I was surprised to find a black pearl in my chin." Song Zhengping said: "In May, Yangmei is full of the forest. At first, I suspected that one piece was worth a thousand gold: the taste is as heavy as grapes from Hebei, and the color is as deep as lychee from the south." (He also said: "The salt in Yangmei can be removed." Yangmei is rich in fruit acid, which can help digestion in the stomach and intestines, but it is harmful to the tooth magnet, so it is suitable to eat it with salt. Li Bai's poem says: "Yangmei in the jade plate is set up for you, and the Wu salt is as white as snow. Hold the salt and drink the wine, and don't learn from Yi and Qi to be noble." It can be seen that Yangmei has been eaten with salt for a long time. Yang Chengzhai said: "Jade skin is half drunk with red millet, and black halo is slightly dyed with purple bags." These are all good verses about Yangmei.

Worth Introducing Domestic Factories (4)

— He Gongxing

(5) Ice-Making Factories

There are about ten ice-making factories in Shanghai. Among those opened by Chinese people, there are three relatively large ones: Guangye in Gaochang Temple and Qialong on Kang Nao Tuo Road.

And Zhihe in Hongkou, etc. Among those opened by foreigners, there are three British-owned ones: Tongmao and Shanghai Maochang, etc., and one Japanese-owned one: Dongfang. Tongmao is particularly large, producing 35 tons of ice per day. The market price is 15 or 16 yuan per ton.

Ice-making machines are also called refrigerating machines. Smaller ones cost four to five thousand yuan each, while larger ones cost more than ten thousand yuan.

The ice-making time takes about 24 hours. In addition to placing cold water and a small amount of saltwater for isolation, a considerable amount of ammonia is added to the iron pipes next to the machine. This ammonia is an indispensable material for making ice. Ammonia is an American or British product, costing 80 taels of silver per barrel of 100 pounds.

(6) Soda Factories

Soda is a summer beverage. Lemon aids digestion, orange juice strengthens the stomach, sarsaparilla water removes dampness and cleanses the blood, and ginger beer benefits qi and warms the stomach, all of which are beneficial to health. Foreign Zheng Guanghe soda is popular every summer. The industry is characterized by light investment and high profits, and the outflow of profits every year is incalculable. The machinery for making soda includes water-making, sugar-pouring, water-filtering, and bottle-washing equipment. The most difficult aspects are the manufacturing of bottles and the manufacturing of fruit juice. Domestic goods are not suitable for both. It was previously heard that Watson's factory had conducted extensive research on bottles and juice, but still found it difficult to solve. It is hoped that the three types of industrialists mentioned above will conduct mutual research and catch up quickly. Perhaps there will be a chance of success.

The working machinery varies in size and output. Roughly speaking, a water-making machine can produce 1,500 dozen bottles of water per day, and an ice-making machine can produce about 2 tons of ice. Other machines, such as bottle washing machines, filling machines, corking machines, and carbonation machines, are all foreign products.

Among domestic soda factories, Watson's is the largest, having been established for 30 years. In May of the 13th year of the Republic of China, it was taken over by Chinese people. The capital is 300,000 yuan. Last year's business totaled 240,000 yuan. The next largest are Yili, Huisi, and Shesheng, totaling four companies.

Casual Talk

— Liusha

Rotten Banknotes: If foreign bank notes issued by foreign banks are old or damaged, the banks often exchange them for new ones. Only Chinese banknotes, once issued, continue to circulate endlessly until the bank collapses. Even if they are moldy, the patterns are blurred, they are as broken as spider webs, and the accumulated dirt is as thick as oilcloth, no one cares. Recently, a medical student accidentally took a banknote and examined it under a microscope and surprisingly discovered more than 36,000 microbes on it. It is said that these microbes are all poisonous and can transmit diseases to people.

Wine and Tobacco: In the world, the country with the most people who drink alcohol is Belgium. There is a wine shop for every thirty-six people. The country with the most opium smokers in the world is China. The people walking on the streets are all thin and pale, and recently they are going to implement a public opium sale.

Africans: People always think that Africans are born black, born black from their mother’s womb. This sounds correct, but it is actually a big mistake. African children are born white, but within a year they turn purple, and then they get darker day by day, until they become completely black by the time they are thirty years old.

After Watching the Movie "Kind Mother"

— Jiang Shoubo

Comparing the silent film "(Kind Mother)" by the Star Film Company with the Western film of the same name, the situation is naturally different, but there is one point that I admire the company's success very much, and that is in terms of makeup. Yan Yuexian, she is a plump and fat person, with a lot of meat on her face. Her original appearance is quite youthful and beautiful. Now in the play, she can transform into an old woman with wrinkled skin and white hair. Even her walking, speaking, and every move still maintain her physical condition. It is very difficult.

Gu Meijun, she is skilled in Peking Opera, but since joining Star, she has only appeared once in "(Silver Star Lucky)," which seems a bit awkward. Here, I feel that Meijun has made rapid progress. In court, she pleads for Jia Haiquan, speaking eloquently, with a lively demeanor, very capable of showing Feng Gu's ability. The scene on the riverbank in the countryside has a beautiful scenery, making it the crown of the whole play.

Wang Xianzai's Jia Haiquan is divided into three periods. At first, he is a bad guy, but in prison, he has already repented somewhat. Later, influenced by his virtuous mother and good wife, he also becomes a kind person. Xianzai's performance in these three periods is truly masterful.

Tang Jie's Feng Da, Wang Weixin's Cao Si, and Huang Junpu's village teacher are all mediocre. Huang Junpu's comical performance is based on his naturally strange face, but it is a pity that he has lost a lot of weight now.

As for the overall compilation of the play, Cheng Xiaoqing was able to use his clever mind to direct it, making it very intense and moving. Zhang Shichuan directed it without losing the original meaning, and he was especially able to use small actions to enhance its spirit. When I watch domestic films, I am unwilling to praise too much. I feel quite satisfied with this one "(Kind Mother)."

Records of Knocking on the Ancient Temple Bell (49)

— Bu Chu Ting Cao Zhai Fu

Fifty-three

Strangely enough, Mr. Zhu's problem is no longer a problem. These days, no one has mentioned his failing the exam. Even Old Xu himself is in the stick team, enthusiastically drilling. Zhang Bearded doesn't know how he came back and is smoking his opium under the protection of the peasants' armed forces. He is over the age for compulsory military training, so he doesn't have to drill or keep watch. He has actually become the most comfortable person in our village.

Fifty-four

The good day for the start of school 丨March 15丨 arrived. The children, dressed in fresh new clothes, came very early one by one. They seemed as happy as during the New Year. Indeed, this is a new era in their life history. Whether they have already anticipated it themselves, I can only understand if I am reborn as a child.

Regimental Commander Chunsheng issued an order saying that today's first school opening is a major event in the village, and all members must participate in the opening ceremony in full armor. For a time, the rifle team, shotgun team, sword team, knife team, spear team, and stick team, plus the temporary hoe team and sickle team, totaled two hundred people, lined up, blowing drums, and setting off firecrackers, marching around the village to the ancient temple. Mr. Zhu and Battalion Commander Jiang said that such a solemn and majestic school opening had never been seen before. When the people's schools in the city open, they sometimes find a few Boy Scouts to help or hire a military band to boost the atmosphere, but that is just for show. But today, what we have personally seen is that all the children in the village are going to school under the armed protection of their own people. The meaning contained in this is immeasurably rich.

Hu Nan: Approximately fifteen or sixteen boats arrived yesterday from various routes. Port storage is gradually increasing, while retail and door-to-door sales are decreasing. The market for thick japonica rice has also fallen by a few cents. Although the arrival of early and late rice is scarce, prices have also fallen by a few cents.

Xin Zha: The number of boats arriving on the western route yesterday was limited. However, there was still a large influx of Changshu, Xixi, and Jiangyin Yixing rice. Trading in this area is slow, with list prices down by 20 cents. There is some limited demand for early rice from rural villages. The market for foreign Du Jian rice is slow and weak. The market for converted silver dollars is weak due to cloudy weather. Fortunately, inventory is low, so there is little fluctuation in the market.

Northern Merchant Groups Continue to Purchase Foreign Rice

There is discussion within the association to maintain prices.

The foreign rice market continued to weaken yesterday. Small-grain rice continued to fall by a few cents. Demand in this area remains slow. However, Northern merchant groups from Tianjin and other ports, considering the repeated declines in the Shanghai market, found it profitable to purchase over 2,000 bags of small-grain rice. Local retailers also purchased a small amount of small-grain rice, in addition to 200 bags of Saigon rice, at prices slightly lower than last week. The Rice Industry Association had discussions yesterday to maintain prices, but no viable solution has been reached.

Flour trading will only be conducted during the morning session from July 13th to August 3rd.

Yesterday, after the opening bell in the flour market, prices for all months showed a fluctuating trend. Foreign wheat prices fell by another one or two cents. However, supply was very limited, and major factories were hesitant to sell, resulting in very quiet trading. Only over 30,000 bags were traded in the morning. Tianjin deliveries are still priced at 1 tael, 2 mace, 9 qian, and 1 fen. As a result, sentiment improved, and subsequent sales may continue at current levels, or prices may stabilize. As a result, July prices rose by two cents from the previous day, August prices rose by one cent and two and a half li, September and October prices rose by one cent, and November and December prices rose by one cent and two and a half li. Furthermore, the Flour Exchange, due to the recent hot weather, in accordance with past practice and at the request of all members, decided that from the 13th of this month to the 3rd of August, only the morning session will be held. The afternoon session will be canceled. However, the morning session will be changed to open at 9:30 AM and will include three additional sessions, for a total of six sessions.

Extra Local Edition of Shen Bao

Commentary

The Truth About Suicide (Continued)

— Buddhist

Yesterday, I rambled on and on about the truth of suicide. In fact, if my suggestions were implemented, it would definitely reduce the youth's anxiety and the number of suicides. Because I still have more to say, I will add a few more words today.

Economic oppression and love problems are indeed two separate things, but there is a strong causal relationship between them. Because I am someone who has suffered from this experience, I have struggled for decades under the condition of economic oppression, and it is still unresolved. I feel personally and deeply. Now, students in general universities or middle schools also have this trend. Before they have finished their studies, everyone is desperately talking about freedom and love, putting the subjects they should be studying behind them. This is a big mistake and a big misunderstanding.

Do you want to fall in love? Today, I will use two ancient people as examples. Suppose you achieve the goal of love and encounter such a situation, how would you feel and what would you do? It's a dead end. Zhu Maichen of the Han Dynasty was poor and loved to read. He often sold firewood to support himself, reading as he walked. His wife was ashamed and left him. Maichen said, "I will be rich and noble when I am fifty. You have suffered for a long time. When I am rich, I will repay you." His wife said, "If I wait for you to be rich, I will have starved to death long ago." She did not listen and went to marry a farmer.

Also, Wang Zhang of the Han Dynasty, when he was a student, studied in Chang'an and lived alone with his wife. Zhang was sick and had no quilt, lying in a cowhide coat, crying and saying goodbye to his wife. His wife scolded him angrily.

Suppose you marry a modern girl but don't have the ability to make a living and encounter such a situation, would you be painful or not? Can you endure it or not? Not only that, the ancients said, "One person becomes twice as difficult, two people become three times easier." After love, the crystallizations of love, Big Brother, Second Brother, Third Brother... are manufactured one by one from the manufacturing plant, making your burden heavier day by day and your pain deeper day by day. This is truly as Mr. Yu Youren said, "It's hard to get by."

As the children gradually grow up, let them go to school. How can you afford such aristocratic schools? If you don't give them some education, will you teach the crystallization of love to become bandits, hooligans, or bums? Moreover, in this day and age, even if they are good citizens, they are either sent in batches to the enemy's artillery fire or to their own warlord's artillery fire. What is the meaning of creating citizens? Leaving aside this, food, clothing, shelter, and transportation are enough for you to suffer.

Even if your son is raised to be intelligent and successful, becoming an official or a rich man, it is your son and daughter-in-law who are happy. What does it have to do with you, the old man? Suppose you embrace the principle of celibacy. Because of celibacy, life will definitely be less oppressive. Moreover, the celibacy I advocate is not absolute, but relative. Suppose you have the ability to make a living and have a stable job, then you can transform celibacy into dual-personism, which is not impossible. Moreover, the current marriage system is unreliable. As the saying goes, "A farmer who harvests ten more bushels of wheat still wants to change wives." You see, nowadays, those so-called important people, because they have suddenly become officials, either divorce or abandon their former humble wives and pursue a modern girl to fulfill their duties. According to my suggestion, you can also save a divorce procedure. Why be afraid not to do it?

Sending to Friends in Sorrow

— Zhou Dayang

The day before yesterday, I suddenly received a letter from my friend Zhou Dayang, and when I opened it, it was several drafts of poems. I am submitting them to this journal for the enjoyment of fellow enthusiasts. Zeye adds a note:

What is the matter with a man weeping,

Counting the past is more like a dream,

I pity the lotus picking side by side,

I resent the willow's confusing eyes,

The hidden pain of a thousand years is the same,

The two words heartbreaking is what to do,

A little infatuation, a little tear,

Arrange the sea of ​​hate to brew the waves of love.

I once pawned my sable fur to buy spring,

I kept the affair of roasting my calf nose,

I believe that with intention, hate will eventually be near,

Loving the other half makes it easy to worry,

Disturbing a hundred feelings with wind and rain,

Accompany me with double demons and sickness,

Knowing that the oath of the same hole has been felt,

Difficult to fulfill the wish of the earth and the sky.

Studies

How to Make Cod Liver Oil

— Yingzhou

Cod liver oil is something that, when taken, can nourish blood and treat the lungs, and its effect is very great. In recent years, it has been sold in the country in large quantities, mostly imported products. The outflow of profits is deeply lamented. According to the raw materials for this oil, which are taken from the livers of croakers (that is, croaker fish), are very abundant in Shidao, Shandong, China. It was originally a waste product discarded by fishermen when they salt-cured croakers. If you want to collect raw materials, you don't need any capital. Therefore, I deeply hope that ambitious entrepreneurs will go to purchase and imitate it, and also revitalize national goods. I will introduce the manufacturing method as follows.

(A) Cooking Method

This method directly puts a large amount of raw materials into a pot, slowly heats and cooks them, the oil that melts out is drawn from the side, and the residue is taken out from time to time, and new raw materials are put in for continuous work. Finally, the residue is pressed to squeeze out the remaining oil. The fuel used in this method must be firewood. If coal is used, the heat will be too intense, and the oil will be colored by scorching. Using firewood can avoid this concern.

(B) Refining Method: There are several methods for this method, and the commonly used ones are listed as follows.

(1) Washing Method The oil obtained contains a large amount of impurities, namely protein, mucus, dust, etc., which generate bad odors and are prone to decay. Therefore, after collecting it, a large amount of water must be added and stirred for washing. After standing, the oil will appear as a transparent layer. This layer is drawn out and then water is added again. This can be repeated several times to obtain transparent oil.

(2) Standing Method The oil is injected into a container and left to stand for a long time. The impurities will settle, and the oil will form a transparent layer. Draw it out to obtain transparent oil. Also, inject the oil into a shallow container and expose it to direct sunlight. Standing for a long time will not cause changes in the oil, but the impurities will be acidified and decomposed, gradually bleaching, which is also effective.

(3) Filtration Method This method is the most common method, that is, the bleached and standing oil is drawn out according to the method described above, and passed through layers of filter paper and charcoal powder. When filtering, more transparent oil can be obtained. Recently, sand and clay are mixed into the oil, heated slightly to absorb odors or impurities, and then filtered again to obtain better results.

(4) Refining Method by Adding Acid When sulfuric acid is added to the oil, the salts become sulfates and dissolve other dirt, which is carbonized and precipitated. Although sulfuric acid has a strong effect on oil, a small amount can have a special refining effect. About 1% is diluted in water of equal volume, added, and heated to a low temperature. If there is dirt precipitation, remove it. The oil is washed with clean water until it does not show an acid reaction.

Family Topics

It's Reversed, It's Reversed

— Iwa no

Mrs. Jin has been saying "It's reversed, it's reversed" to people recently. People don't understand the meaning of her "It's reversed, it's reversed." They want to ask her for clarification, but they don't dare to open their mouths because of her frosty and angry look.

One day last week, Mrs. Wang from the eastern neighborhood held a soup cake feast for her one-month-old son. Mrs. Jin, out of the friendship of many years of neighbors, went to congratulate her and was invited to be a guest of honor. Most of the people at the table were acquaintances, eating, laughing, and talking. They unconsciously started talking about daughters-in-law. As soon as Mrs. Jin talked about daughters-in-law, she immediately blurted out "It's reversed, it's reversed" again. Old Mrs. Shen at the same table had wanted to ask her what "It's reversed, it's reversed" meant for a long time. Today was a good opportunity, so she couldn't easily miss it, so she took the opportunity to say, "Mrs. Jin, what is 'It's reversed, it's reversed'? You've been saying it for a long time. What does it mean?" Mrs. Jin also felt that it was necessary to pour out this secret today, so she restrained her smile and said, "My son and my daughter-in-law got engaged last year. This year, in the midst of the gunfire, they were hastily married. Although the gunfire was shocking, I was happy to have completed my son's marriage. Because it was affected by the war, everything was frugal, so a maid was not hired. Everyone at home does things themselves. When the new daughter-in-law first arrived, everyone was very polite, so I didn't want her to do anything. I took care of all the things like washing clothes and cooking myself. I didn't want her to worry or work hard. I carried the food to the table one by one, and then went to call her and my son out to eat. After everyone had eaten, I carried everything back, put it away, and washed it. She and my son had already gone to their room. After a week, I felt that I had to speak up, but the new daughter-in-law was still polite after all, and I was embarrassed to say it to her face, so I called my son over and secretly told him, 'I am also over fifty years old, and I have always been served by servants, and I am used to being comfortable. Now we are trying to save money and not hire a maid, but we have added a daughter-in-law. I didn't want the daughter-in-law to serve me. I only ask her to help me with my work. Now a week has passed, and I think I will ask her to take charge of the housework tomorrow. If she says she is inexperienced, then I will guide her in everything.' You go and tell her that I will definitely hand over the work tomorrow." The son didn't reply that day. At ten o'clock the next morning, their door was still tightly closed, and they were sleeping soundly. I thought that if I went any later, there wouldn't be any good goods in the small vegetable market, so I went to buy vegetables myself. Their door was also open. I called my son out and said to him, 'The vegetables have been bought. Tell your daughter-in-law to come and pick and wash them quickly!' I deliberately raised my voice a little, thinking that she would definitely hear it and come out. Who knew that as soon as I finished speaking, a voice even louder than mine came from the room: 'I can't cook. I haven't learned how to cook. I can't serve people either. I'm used to being served.' To maintain harmony in the family, I swallowed my anger and continued to do the work myself. To this day, this burden is still pressing on my shoulders. With a mother-in-law serving her daughter-in-law and a mother serving her son like this, isn't it reversed? What is it?"

When Mrs. Jin said this, everyone sighed deeply. Old Mrs. Shen asked again, "If your daughter-in-law eats and does nothing, then what does she do?" Mrs. Jin said again, "She is busier than me! Every morning, she gets up after ten o'clock and asks my son to make water for her to wash her face. She looks in the mirror, puts on powder, draws her eyebrows, and dyes her nails. She is busy for an hour. After resting for a while, she wants to eat. After putting down her bowl, she washes her face, puts on powder, draws her eyebrows, and dyes her nails again. After everything is done, she either goes out for a walk with my son or plays mahjong at home. She doesn't go to bed until twelve o'clock at night. This is their daily routine." Old Mrs. Shen asked again, "What kind of family is she from?" Mrs. Jin said, "She is a female student who studies at some middle school. She hasn't graduated yet. Because she came to my house, she doesn't go to school anymore. I really don't understand. If girls read books and can't even do some things at home, then what's the use of reading these books?"

Casual Talk

Random Notes While Sweating

— Xin

(1)

When you are drunk and full, the most suitable thing for you to do is to lean in the arms of your poetic lover and say in a trembling voice: "My love, how empty life is!"

But when you are not only not drunk but also full, you must remember that this sentence is useless to you. Because the suffering of "life is empty" is ultimately not as painful as "an empty belly."

(2)

A poet wakes up from a half-night's dream, looks at the cold moonlight shining on the window, gets up, pours a cup of cold tea from the night before, and drinks it. The taste is astringent and slightly bitter, so he sighs and says:

"Oh, your cold tea from the night before,

Is a symbol of the bitter life!"

Looking at the moon, the moon is still so cold, and the four walls are so silent that there is no echo. The poet finally collapses and falls down. Before long, poetic snoring is heard again.

(3)

Tiny green worms see the light and fly in groups from outside the window to my desk. I stab them to death one by one with a pen. In an instant, a large pile of remains is piled up. Under this game of life, I feel the pride of the victor and the sorrow of the loser!

But who told them to head towards the light? Shouldn't the green worms?

(4)

In the evening, suddenly dark clouds rose, strong winds blew, lightning flashed and thunder roared, followed by heavy rain. A black dog trembled in the wind and rain, miserable. A silly child said: "Dog, where are you going to escape?"

(5)

Every time I walk through Nanjing Road, I never dare to raise my head, because I am afraid of seeing the chaotic "human beasts" rushing around. I am afraid of seeing the cars carrying flesh and blood rushing around in groups. However, looking at the ground, the ground also seems to be covered with blood and flesh. I have to close my eyes. Sparks fly in front of my eyes, and I vaguely see landmines buried all over the ground!

I think these landmines will explode one day!

Car

The Fallacious Views of Modern Women

— Jin Nan

Now, most women think that dressing fashionably means being a new woman? With such a huge misconception, many women put effort into dressing up, focusing on Europeanization, in order to win the title of a new woman and get praise from men. In this situation, new women become special parasites who neither serve society nor devote themselves to their families. They not only eat their fill all day long and do nothing, but also constantly ask their husbands or parents for money, wearing luxurious clothes, putting on heavy makeup, watching movies, going to boring banquets, and making social interactions like showy prostitutes. It's most funny. They blindly shout the high-pitched rhetoric of women's liberation, but on the one hand, they are reversing the car of lowering their own status. Just talking about the many women who have received a new education, how many can be economically independent, how many can have a happy marriage, how many can improve the family environment, how many can make a little contribution to society, and how many can fulfill a responsibility to the country?

We should not generally and so seriously accuse the general fashionable new women or new women who worship material civilization. It is definitely not insulting women, but an objective theory, and at the same time, it is a great worry for those who seek to improve women's rights!

Finally, I would like to express my sincere hope that new women (don't be new in form,

But to be new in spirit.)

Nonsense Dialogue

Dialogue

— Meng Yuan

Bridesmaid: (When you were walking down the aisle, your expression seemed very uneasy, as if you were a little frightened. Bride: (It's my first time doing this, so I can't help but feel a little nervous. I'll have to be more careful next time.)

Man: (Beautiful flowers, sweet candy, these are great ways to increase love.)

Woman: (Hey! Isn't the ring a good thing?)

Employee: (Manager, I'm married now, which has increased my burden. Can you please give me a raise?)

Manager: (The troubles caused outside the store are not related to the store.)

Man: (Honey! Please don't wear lipstick on your lips in the future.)

Woman: (Why???...)

Man: (Because when I went back last night, my wife found out that I had kissed you!)

Market News

The Fuli Photographic Materials Company, located at the intersection of Avenue Joffre and Hualong Road in this city, opened for business yesterday. Its internal organization is unique in Shanghai. In addition to selling all kinds of photographic materials, it also sells used photographic lenses and boxes from various countries at 80% new condition. The prices are only 20% of the original price, making them the cheapest lenses and boxes in the world. It also provides free developing and repair services to customers. Therefore, buyers are very enthusiastic.

The Chinese Chess Company Expansion: The Chinese Chess Company on Wuhua Road in Hongkou has been established for several years. All of its products sell well at home and abroad, and its reputation is outstanding. Now, a department specializing in educational toys is being set up to meet social needs. However, due to insufficient space, the main factory will be moved this year to Renxing Li, at the intersection of Broadway Road and Zhao Feng Road.

Shanghai Local Court

▲Criminal Judgment: Ye Fusheng Theft Case (Main Text) Ye Fusheng is sentenced to six months in prison for theft at the station. The number of days of detention shall be used to offset the prison sentence at a rate of two days for one day. ▲Wen Youguang Opium Case (Main Text) Wen Youguang is sentenced to six months in prison and fined 300 yuan for possessing opium with the intention of selling it. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, it shall be converted to detention at a rate of one yuan per day. The number of days of detention shall be used to offset the prison sentence at a rate of two days for one day. 158 taels of opium are confiscated. ▲Li Jianzhi Opium Case (Main Text) Li Jianzhi is sentenced to six months in prison and fined 60 yuan for providing premises for others to smoke opium with the intention of profiting. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, it shall be converted to detention at a rate of one yuan per day. The number of days of detention shall be used to offset the prison sentence at a rate of two days for one day. Four opium pipes, two opium lamps, eighty red pills, one opium skewer, and a small box of red pill ash are confiscated. ▲Huang Zhimin Embezzlement Case (Main Text) Huang Zhimin is sentenced to three months in prison for embezzling property of others in his possession in the course of his duties with the intention of illegally possessing it for himself. The number of days of detention shall be used to offset the prison sentence at a rate of two days for one day. ▲Liu Shoujian and others Malfeasance Case (Main Text) Liu Shoujian, Liu Fusheng, Wu Shuji, and Qiao Yuchun are acquitted. ▲Zhou Chengshu and others Assault Case (Main Text) Zhou Chengshu and Zhou Shijun are acquitted. ▲Tian Liujin and others Assault Case (Main Text) This public prosecution is not accepted.

▲Public Notice of Service: Hu Shangsheng versus Chen Wanfu for rent arrears. (Main Text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 188 yuan in silver dollars for rent and shall immediately vacate the house. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲Tang Saishu versus Chen Min for debt. (Main Text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff's debt of 2,551 taels and 8 qian and 9 fen in standard silver, plus interest at a rate of 5% per annum from March 1, 1931, until the date of execution. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲Ruling: Yuansheng Money Shop versus Chen Hongfei Loan Application for Provisional Attachment (Main Text) The defendant's share capital of 1,600 taels in Quanfu Public Company should be subject to the creditor's application for provisional attachment. The debtor may request a suspension or cancellation if they provide collateral equal to the original debt amount. The application costs shall be borne by the debtor. ▲The above is to inform the defendant Chen Hongfei. ▲Chen Youmei versus Dong A'xing and others for a Guarantee Case (Main Text) The defendant Dong A'xing shall pay the plaintiff a loan of 215 yuan in silver dollars, plus statutory interest calculated at 5% per annum from the date of the loan agreement until the date of execution. If he is unable to repay, the defendant Zhu Fugeng shall be responsible for repayment. The defendant Jin Xingsheng shall pay the plaintiff a loan of 50 yuan in silver dollars, plus interest calculated at 1.2% per annum from the date of the loan agreement until the date of execution. If he is unable to repay, the defendant Zhu Fugeng shall be responsible for repayment. The plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected. Two-fifths of the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant Dong A'xing, one-fifth by the defendant Jin Xingsheng, and two-fifths by the plaintiff. (Above, July 12)
